National Government Holds Commemoration of the Third Anniversary of Establishing Nanjing as Capital 61

Today (the 18th) is the third anniversary of the National Government establishing Nanjing as its capital. Shops and residences in Nanjing hung national flags to celebrate. The National Government held a commemorative ceremony in the auditorium at 10:00 AM. Attendees included Hu Hanmin, Tan Yankai, Wang Chonghui, Gu Yingfen, Wang Zhengting, Zhang Nanxian, and other officials from the National Government's military and civil service departments, as well as senior officials from various departments, totaling more than 600 people. The order of the ceremony was as follows: (1) All stand at attention; (2) Music is played; (3) The Party song is sung; (4) Three bows are made to the Party and national flags and the portrait of the Generalissimo; (5) Chairman Hu reads the Generalissimo's will; (6) The chairman delivers a speech, stating that Chairman Chiang was unable to attend due to an inspection of the Boy Scouts, and Chairman Tan was not well enough to speak, so he (Hu) would say a few words. Since 1927, the nation and the international community have recognized that the divided and turbulent China ruled by warlords has been unified by the Kuomintang through revolutionary force. Three years ago today, during a time of military urgency, we resolutely and unanimously advocated for establishing Nanjing as the capital. The reasons were: (1) The Generalissimo had decided to make Nanjing the capital after the revolution in 1912, and we should follow his instructions and establish the capital in Nanjing; (2) Every country must move its capital to a new location after major reforms to avoid being infected by old and bad habits, as seen in the recent examples of Russia and Turkey; (3) Nanjing has the qualifications to be a capital in terms of history, transportation, industry, commerce, and culture. Everyone knows that Ankara, the new capital of Turkey, initially had a population of only tens of thousands, and even though it has been the capital for seven or eight years, the population is still not very large, and many construction projects are still in their infancy. However, from a revolutionary standpoint, we should admire them very much. The difficulties of building a capital in Nanjing are less than those in Ankara, and it is also a place designated by the Generalissimo, so we should work hard to achieve our goal of building a perfect capital in the short term. Some people still do not understand, thinking that the capital is not important, and that Nanjing is good, but other places are also possible. This is a big mistake. It must be understood that the capital of a country is like the brain of a person. All undertakings must rely on it to lead. Guangzhou in the south, and Beiping and Xi'an in the north, must be reorganized and built, but everything should have priorities. The best area of a country should naturally be built up as soon as possible. The Capital Construction Committee has now decided on a very good overall construction plan, and in the future, it will be up to us to implement it diligently. I hope that after our capital is completed, it will be comparable to the famous capitals of Europe and America. There are still some stubborn people who do not recognize the big picture, always thinking that people from a certain province should go back to that province and work hard, and that building the capital is not important. This is also a big mistake and should be corrected. In recent years, our efforts have not fully achieved our goals or satisfied the wishes of the people, but we have always followed the Generalissimo's instructions, and there has been some progress and success in education, politics, law, and other aspects. This is something we can be proud of, but no matter what, we are still far from our predetermined goals and must not be complacent. We should work even harder to complete our revolutionary mission in the short term. Hu concluded his speech, followed by music, photography, and adjournment.

Central Propaganda Department Issues Letter of Encouragement to Comrades Trapped in the North 62

The Central Propaganda Department issued a letter of encouragement to comrades trapped in the North today (the 18th), stating: "Since the founding of the Republic of China, the people have suffered and groaned under the division and devastation of feudal warlords for more than ten years. Thanks to the Generalissimo of our Party for calling for struggle in the past, and the continued efforts of all comrades in the future, we were finally able to eliminate the huge and stubborn Northern Warlords and unify our Republic of China. The Central Government, in accordance with the revolutionary program, rigorously implemented political tutelage and construction, hoping that unity would be permanently guaranteed and the people's hardships would be slightly alleviated. Unexpectedly, in the past year, disasters and chaos have repeatedly occurred. Rebellions by Gui, Zhang, Feng, Tang, and other rebels occurred successively, betraying the Party and the country, causing the smooth progress of political tutelage and construction to be hindered, and the people throughout the country suffered from upheaval and displacement again. However, with the loyalty and bravery of our revolutionary soldiers and the joint efforts of all comrades, they were finally put out in the shortest possible time. The successive defeats of these old and new warlords are enough to enlighten the stubborn military personnel. However, Yan Xishan's rebellious ambitions have not died, and he is prone to chaos by nature. Without learning from the past, he is willing to be Feng Yuxiang's successor. He first issued fallacious remarks to confuse the public, and then implemented betrayal, destroying unity, recruiting corrupt remnants, colluding with imperialists, mobilizing troops, and invading southward in multiple routes. He has already isolated himself from the Party and the country and the people. His rebellious acts are obvious and he cannot escape punishment. Our comrades in the North have embraced our ideology, and their faith is unwavering. Motivated by their enthusiasm for protecting the Party and loving the country, they have severely condemned Yan's heresies and atrocities, and have also printed and distributed publications, striving to publicize and clarify the central government's peaceful objectives and correct the views of the people throughout the country. As a result, they have been repeatedly subjected to Yan's oppression, their speech has been suppressed, their actions have lost freedom, arrests have occurred one after another, and prisons have been filled. Our comrades, who have been protecting the Party and the country, have been subjected to oppression, and we feel deeply grateful and saddened. However, our comrades in the North have not been discouraged or intimidated by this. Even under the pressure of Yan's oppressive power, they have continued to make relentless efforts in the spirit of the Generalissimo's great fearlessness, denouncing and demanding punishment. This spirit of unwavering bravery and continued sacrifice and struggle is not only enough to chill the rebels but also enough to inspire the hearts of the people throughout the country, making them aware that revolution and counter-revolution cannot coexist, and that only such sacrifice and struggle can eliminate the obstacles to political tutelage and complete the great cause of revolution. It is therefore that our comrades in the North have made sacrifices and struggled today for an unparalleled glorious price. The central government offers comfort to our comrades for this reason. Yan combines corruption and evil in one furnace, plotting one last attempt. Although his strength is not enough to shake the central government or harm the Party and the country, his resistance is still enough to prolong the war and increase the suffering of the people. The swift eradication of the last warlords and the complete realization of the national revolution depend on the greater sacrifice and struggle of all comrades. If comrades have any thoughts of fear or complacency at this time, not only will the eradication of this remaining vestige of the Northern Warlords be hopeless, but all the already fallen warlords and the remaining counter-revolutionary forces will also rekindle, and all past sacrifices and struggles will be in vain, and the people throughout the country will once again fall into the heavy siege of feudal warlords' division and oppression, which cannot be resolved. Therefore, at this time of the final showdown between revolution and counter-revolution, all our comrades must raise the spirit of great fearlessness and make the greatest determination and sacrifice in order to achieve a sweeping victory, eliminate the root of reaction forever, ensure the unity of the country, so that the people's livelihood can be constructed smoothly, and the political tutelage can be realized as scheduled. Our revolutionary comrades in the North were the vanguard of the May Fourth and March 18th Revolutions, and have long struggled under the feudal forces in the North. Their spirit of sacrificing for the Party has long been recognized by the people of the country. At a time when the remnants of the Northern Warlords and the remaining counter-revolutionaries are encircling our Party, they must reaffirm the history and personality of the revolution, uphold the spirit of the past, and make the final battle. The full success of the revolution lies in this one action. May our comrades in the North encourage each other."

Central Propaganda Department Hosts Press Conference 63

▲ Wu Zhihui Reports on His Thoughts on the Current Situation

The Central Propaganda Department hosted a press conference in the Second Conference Hall of the Central Committee at 2:00 PM on the 17th, with about 20 reporters stationed in Nanjing and from Shanghai, Wuhan, Peiping, Tianjin, and other places. Liu Lu Yin presided over the meeting. After the opening ceremony, he introduced Wu Zhihui, a member of the Central Supervisory Committee, who made the following report:

"I have been busy for days and have not had time to pay attention to the so-called current situation. I will only offer a few of my thoughts from the past few days for your amusement. Now we are in a period of military rule again. Why has this period reappeared? According to my personal thoughts, I will briefly state one or two points. When I went to the North last winter, I had no idea that there would be any military affairs, because Yan Xishan is not a person with any ambition. As for someone occupying territory, it can be forgiven, because he wants to show off his skills and must have a place for him to experiment. Judging from the past situation in Shanxi, he seemed to be cautious and had some political interest. It is also good to have a place for him to experiment. But later, when I went to the North, I saw that he was secretly manipulating everything. The Central Government gave him political responsibility for the provinces of Hebei, Chahar, and Suiyuan, and he himself thought that Shanxi Province alone was not enough to develop his talents, and ambition was born. On the one hand, it is said that he is occupying territory. On the other hand, it can also be said that he is the key to the northern gate. If he does not cause trouble and the northern provinces are entrusted to him, it is not a big deal. If he can really be the key to the northern gate, it is already hard enough for him. So his words are very satisfying. If everyone trusts each other, it will be fine. In reality, no matter which aspect, when the burden has not yet been picked up, one feels very confident. Once it is picked up, one becomes very dissatisfied. Since he is openly opposed, he will naturally have to put on a show on stage. It is inevitable that he will mess things up beyond repair. If he continues to experiment like this, when will it end? It should be known that the people will sometimes not allow them to experiment. Moreover, now there is no way out. There is no time for war. Feng Yuxiang is still performing operas in Shaanxi. In fact, there is not even a blade of grass left in Shaanxi. Who is really saving the country and the people, and who is not wearing a mask? If this continues non-stop, we really dare not make a dogmatic judgment, and we really cannot do it. It is best if they themselves can wake up. All the ugliness of the past does not need to be said to each other. It would be good if everyone could be a little satisfied. The Chinese people love peace. When the time comes, they will also rise up and say, "The revolution has taken away our lives. Please take a rest." Last year, I told him this idea, and he and Mr. Zhao Cilon were very supportive. So far, Mr. Zhao is a little embarrassed and takes a passive attitude. What we don't understand most is the current state of being neither dead nor alive. The Japanese are playing a trick, sometimes helping A against B. When A is about to succeed, they use C against A. If C can succeed, they use another person against C. They are always unwilling to let people succeed. Since they have the strength, they could have made a decisive victory, but they did not come up with this plan, so the current situation in the North has become what it is. Since our Party's Northern Expedition and unification, what we have seen is that key figures should be brought together to the Central Committee, making the Central Committee the Central Committee of everyone. In this situation, stability can be announced. Therefore, after the Tangshan Conference in Beiping, all the key figures gathered in Nanjing and had the sincerity to jointly seek peace. However, Feng Yuxiang showed off his films of the Northwest Army at the Lixingshe, showing his power, which was contrary to the path of peace. As a result, the principle of "Two Greats" was formed. You look down on me, I look down on you. That is the intention. It seems that these films should not be taken out to let people know what the intention is. Before long, everyone felt uncomfortable. So Feng Yuxiang left in January last year. With this departure, he did not want to cooperate, and then ran to the place where the swords and soldiers met. The Guangxi guys are nothing special. May I ask, now that everyone is planning construction, what do they still need soldiers for? The reason why they still want soldiers is that there are a few Chinese sayings, "The beauty of the palace, the service of concubines, the poor people I know have obtained me." Because the poor people I know have obtained me, they are unwilling to cut the soldiers. They will rule one day at a time. Unfortunately, the Guangxi people drove away Lu Dipin, the chairman of Hunan. At that time, Hu Zongduo and Tao Jun were very angry and unwilling to admit their mistakes. Then they even opened fire. Feng Yuxiang first

Indeed, he had some tricks with the Gui faction. At that time, Feng sat on the sidelines, and when Li Zongren and others were defeated, Sun Liangcheng also left Shandong. After the Northwest Army retreated, Zhang Fakui rose up again. When Zhang was in Hubei, the Northwest did not fluctuate, but when Zhang arrived in Hunan, Song Zheyuan, Shi Jingting, and others came out again. These are like joking, simply joking with the people. This kind of rebellion is too unwise, with no purpose at all. We cannot help but sigh. Yan Xichuan now also wants to try it out, seeking the highest position. In fact, what is the method of the highest position? He doesn't understand it at all. What he has seen before is Xu Shichang's set of tricks. He wants to open the door and take a look first. If there is nothing in the east or west, and the civil and military officials are lined up, and when you have no way out, he can swagger out and sit on the dragon throne. Isn't it extremely ridiculous? Liang Zhuoru has a saying that China has too many talents and it is not economical. It is true. Yan Xishan can only be the governor of a province, and Feng Yuxiang can only be a good official. However, they do not do it well and always want to fight, always wanting to be the boss. But turning around and around, they are still a second in command. As for how to be a boss, they don't understand it at all. This is the uneconomical use of talent."

Pre-Decision Points for the Family and Inheritance Sections of the Civil Code (Continued) 64

▲Hu Hanmin and Lin Sen Request the Central Political Council to Decide

(3) Should spouses inherit property? If so, what is their order of succession and what share should they inherit? According to our old laws, there is no clear provision as to whether a husband can inherit his deceased wife's property. If a husband dies without children, a chaste wife may inherit her husband's share, but she must still have the clan leader choose someone of appropriate rank and generation to be an heir, and transfer the inheritance to the future heir. Initially, the wife did not have the right to inherit her husband's property upon his death. In drafting the inheritance law this time, should the spouse of the deceased inherit property? This is the fourth point for preliminary decision. If they are to inherit, what is the order of succession? Foreign laws vary considerably. Some place them in the same order as direct descendants, such as the German and Swiss Civil Codes. Others place them after direct descendants as a secondary heir, such as the Japanese Civil Code. The share to be inherited also varies from country to country. According to the German Civil Code, if the deceased has relatives of the first degree, the spouse of the deceased receives one-quarter of the estate. If there are relatives of the second degree or grandparents, the spouse receives one-half of the estate. If there are grandparents and their direct descendants, the spouse receives one-half, plus the share of the direct descendants. If there are no relatives of the first or second degree, or grandparents, the spouse receives the entire estate. According to the Swiss Civil Code, if the deceased has direct descendants, the spouse may choose to receive either a usufruct of one-half of the estate or full ownership of one-quarter of the estate. If there are parents or their direct descendants, the spouse receives full ownership of one-quarter of the estate and a usufruct of three-quarters. If there are grandparents or their direct descendants, the spouse receives full ownership of one-half of the estate and a usufruct of one-half. If there are no grandparents or their direct descendants, the spouse receives the entire estate. How should our inheritance law be formulated? This is the fifth point for preliminary decision. (4) If, before the commencement of inheritance, an heir has received part of the property from the deceased due to marriage, separation, or business, how should this be calculated when distributing the inheritance? According to our laws on this point, there is no written law to follow. In foreign countries, the value of the gift is added to the value of the property owned by the deceased at the time of inheritance, and this is considered the inheritance property. The calculated share to be inherited is then reduced by the value of the gift, as in the Japanese Civil Code. The Swiss Civil Code is generally similar. How should our inheritance law be formulated? This is the sixth point for preliminary decision. (5) How should the inherited property be distributed among those with the same right to inherit, based on whether they have contributed to the inherited property? According to our old laws, there are no provisions regarding the share to be inherited by an heir who has contributed to the inherited property. The Swiss Civil Code has explicit solutions to this point. A son who is of age and lives with his parents, providing labor or income, may request reasonable compensation when dividing the estate, unless he explicitly waives it. How should our inheritance law be formulated? This is the seventh point for preliminary decision. (6) If guaranteed inheritance portions are to be stipulated, how should they be stipulated? According to our old laws, there are only provisions for inherited shares. The scope of the deceased's right to dispose of property is not clearly defined. Should our inheritance law follow the legislative examples of most countries and stipulate guaranteed inheritance portions? This is the eighth point for preliminary decision. If guaranteed inheritance portions are to be stipulated, what should their scope be? This is also a problem. In Germany, the guaranteed inheritance portion is half the value of the legal inherited share. In Switzerland, direct descendants receive three-quarters of their share, parents receive one-half each, and siblings receive one-quarter each. When the surviving spouse inherits together with other legal heirs, they inherit the entire property. When the spouse is the sole heir, they inherit one-half. In Japan, the rules differ depending on whether the heir is a head of household or an inheritor of property, and also depending on whether they are a direct descendant or not. How should our inheritance law be formulated? This is the ninth point for preliminary decision. (End)

Suppression of Foreign-Licensed Opium Dens in Fujian Province 65

▲Result of Negotiations by the Anti-Opium Association with the Japanese Consulate. Fuzhou Correspondence: Most of the Taiwanese people residing in Fuzhou and Xiamen make a living by opening opium dens and selling opium. Since Fujian Province implemented opium suppression, the opium dens and opium businesses run by Fujianese have been completely banned. The Taiwanese people have seized this opportunity to seek profit alone. In total, there are hundreds of foreign-licensed opium dens and opium businesses in Fuzhou and Xiamen. The harm they cause to society is imaginable. The provincial government has repeatedly negotiated with the Japanese consulate to ban them, but without effect. Recently, the provincial anti-opium committee discovered that the procedures for opening these foreign businesses require Taiwanese people to first report the business name, address, capital, and business type to the Japanese consulate, which then sends personnel to investigate and issue a special license before allowing them to open. However, the majority of foreign businesses that specialize in selling opium have not been formally approved by the consulate. Some have had their licenses revoked but still display them. Others have opened businesses privately without permission. Still others have registered and obtained licenses, but the location of the business does not match the original application, or the name of the business owner or manager does not match the license. Some falsely report their license number and set up multiple branches without displaying goods, privately transferring profits. There are also cases of using expired licenses or false numbers to deceive and replace legitimate businesses, leading to numerous abuses. The committee specifically sent member Shi Ming to visit the Japanese consul in Fuzhou, Tamura Teiichi, requesting that Chinese authorities be allowed to send personnel to search and close down these illegal and informal foreign businesses in conjunction with the Japanese consulate police. The Japanese consul initially made excuses to evade the request, but after repeated arguments by Committee Member Shi, he agreed to comply. However, he said that they would first send personnel to investigate and order the closure of foreign businesses that were found to be illegal. If the Chinese authorities discovered any more illegal businesses, they would then conduct a joint search with the police. Therefore, in recent days, the Japanese consulate has sent many police officers to investigate over thirty businesses, including Baoli Foreign Business on Shanghang Street, and found that they were all engaged in illegal activities and would be suppressed. At the same time, before the joint action with the Japanese police, our side also dispatched detectives from the Municipal Public Security Bureau to station themselves in front of various foreign businesses, specifically waiting for Chinese citizens to enter to smoke opium or buy opium, and then detaining them for investigation. Dozens of people have already been arrested. After this cleanup, the opium haze that pervades Fuzhou may gradually be expected to wane. (April 16)

Important News Two

A Glimpse of Sian's Capture by Bandits 66

▲Military and Police Jointly Attack and Recapture on the 16th

▲Three Bandit Leaders Killed and Over Three Hundred Bandits Killed

Huzhou Correspondence: Bandit gangs in Huzhou Prefecture have been rampant in recent years, especially in the Changxing area, where the situation has become extremely serious. Since the Taihu bandit gangs were suppressed last winter and fled to Changxing, they have joined forces with the remnants of Anhui's Bao Gang and the Big Sword Society, resulting in an increase in their arrogance. Cases of looting villages and kidnapping for ransom occur almost daily. In the past ten days, they have successively confiscated the firearms of the defense corps in more than ten places, including Xucang, Xiayuan, and Dukou in Changxing, and publicly declared that they would attack certain cities and towns on a fixed date. On the 14th of this month, about 5,000 bandits suddenly gathered at Changqiao Pass, the intersection of Si'an and Lincheng Bridge in Changxing, to attack an important town. The bandit situation was dangerous. After receiving the news, the 1st and 2nd Battalions of the 30th Regiment of the 5th National Army stationed nearby, as well as the security team and water police, immediately deployed to suppress them. However, due to the disparity in numbers, more than 2,000 bandits occupied Si'an Town, the commercial center of Changxing, at 8:00 AM on the 15th. After the military and police fought bravely, Si'an was finally recaptured at 8:00 AM on the 16th. The information obtained is summarized as follows:

▲General Bandit Situation: The bandits who plunder various parts of Changxing are generally divided into three major groups: one is the remnants of Bao Gang, one is the Taihu bandit gang, and the other is the Big Sword Society from the Anhui border. In total, they number no less than 5,000 to 6,000 people. On the 7th of this month, these bandits surrounded Guangde County, Anhui, which is very close to Changxing. Fortunately, County Magistrate Zhou personally led the self-defense corps to defend the city, fighting fiercely with the bandits for a day and night, and the siege was lifted. After the bandits were defeated in Guangde, they fled back to Changxing to gather, spread out scouts, confiscated the firearms of the defense corps, and recruited ruffians and local thugs, creating a huge commotion. However, this disorganized crowd is no match for a single blow from the military and police.

▲Attack on Si'an: Si'an is the commercial center of Changxing County. In recent years, it has worked hard on construction, and the municipal administration is quite impressive. Transportation is also very convenient. It takes six hours by steamship to reach Wuxing. Moreover, this area is a rice-producing region, and merchants travel back and forth, year after year. Therefore, it is especially coveted by bandits. On the 14th, several thousand bandits gathered at Changqiao Pass, twenty miles from the town. When the National Army and the security team sent troops to suppress them, the bandits retreated to Si'an. The town's defenses were weak and ineffective, and it was eventually occupied by the bandits at 8:00 AM on the 15th.

▲Occupied for One Day: At 8:00 AM on the 15th, a large group of bandits arrived at Si'an Town. All transportation facilities, such as telephones, were simultaneously cut off from the outside world. Most of the bandits were dressed in short clothes, with some wearing military uniforms like soldiers. The People's Army banners were planted all around the town, and several bandit leaders went to the Chamber of Commerce to demand 100,000 yuan in military expenses. The members of the Chamber of Commerce agreed to pay the money at 2:00 PM on the 16th. The bandit leaders then notified the remaining bandits not to disturb the residents. Therefore, no robbery incidents occurred in the town. The next morning, at 8:00 AM, the National Army and the security team and water police launched attacks from different directions and recaptured the town. In total, the town was occupied by the bandits for twelve hours.

▲Military and Police Attack: When the bandits occupied Si'an, the 1st Battalion of the 30th Regiment of the 5th National Army and the 1st Company of the 2nd Security Regiment stationed there were counterattacked by the bandits and retreated to the Taiping Bridge area. After a fierce battle for an hour, the bandits were no match for the troops, and the troops retreated back to Lincheng Bridge. At that time, Hang Yi, the bandit suppression commander of Huzhou and commander of the 2nd Security Regiment, received an urgent telegram from the area and personally led two platoons of machine gun soldiers on the county government's steamship to Lincheng Bridge on the morning of the 15th. On the way, the ship's machinery broke down, so they turned back and changed to the Jialu warship. However, the rivers in the western countryside are mostly shallow and narrow, making it difficult for the ship to navigate. Therefore, it was already 11:00 AM when they arrived at Lincheng Bridge. He then joined forces with the 1st Battalion of the 30th Regiment of the 5th National Army and the 11th Water Police Team, and commanded the 7th, 8th, 9th, and 3rd Companies of the 2nd Security Regiment to attack the Si'an bandits from the left and right flanks, using mortars to advance. After a fierce battle for five hours, the bandits finally collapsed and withdrew from Si'an. One group fled towards Changqiao Pass, and another group escaped towards Meixi in Anji.

▲Confirmed Number of Deaths: When the military and police jointly suppressed the bandits, the National Army took the left flank, the security team took the right flank, and the water police were in the center. Their momentum was extremely fierce. Therefore, the total number of bandits killed was over 300, and many were captured. More than twenty wooden-shell guns were seized. The military and police also suffered nearly a hundred deaths. Among the bandits killed, three bandit leaders were identified: one was Yu Chengyi (formerly a training officer for the Shaoxing Defense Corps), one was Li Guangxin, and one was Wang Zibin. These three bandits were confirmed to be bandit leaders. It is not yet known whether any other bandit leaders were killed. It is also said that the company commander of the 9th Company of the 2nd Security Regiment went missing during the suppression of the bandits. The truth is not yet clear. Bandit Suppression Commander Hang Yi is currently personally leading troops to pursue the bandits.

▲Wuxing Martial Law: Since the bandit incidents in Changxing occurred one after another, Wuxing, which is very close, has also been under heavy guard. Martial law was declared in the city and countryside yesterday. After the news of Si'an's loss spread, the residents were extremely panicked. They were only calmed by the news of the recapture. The county government and the headquarters of the 2nd Security Regiment, deeply concerned that the bandits wreaking havoc in Changxing might have a political background, have already sent telegrams to the Taihu Bandit Suppression Headquarters and the provincial government, requesting that troops be sent to Huzhou to consolidate the defenses.

The Resolution of Gao Guizi's Troops 67

Jinan Correspondence: Gao Guizi's troops have been besieged for nearly two months since February 20th. Those in Zhucheng were besieged by Fan Xiji of the 46th Division, and those in Juxian were besieged by Chen Yaohan of the 26th Division. Although external support has been cut off, they are still resisting stubbornly. There has not been much fighting in the Juxian area, but there has been fierce fighting in the Zhucheng area. Fan's troops have bravely launched several attacks, but were repelled due to heavy artillery fire. Gao's troops have a commanding position on the city, and are protected by the city walls, giving them a significant advantage. Recently, representatives of the Zhucheng people, Pei Mingyu and Zhang Yanyuan, came to Jinan to meet with Chen Diaoyuan, the chairman of the provincial government, requesting a cessation of attacks and a peaceful resolution of the Gao troops, in order to avoid harming the people in the city. Chen indicated that as long as Gao Guizi obeyed the central government, it would be acceptable. The representatives then went from Jinan to Juxian to meet with Gao Guizi to discuss the matter. As a result, Gao agreed to send a telegram to the central government, declaring that he was still willing to serve the party and the country. The other day, Guo Nianzhen, a staff officer of the General Staff Department, and Jiang Huiruo and Cao Jiqing, representatives of Ma Hongkui, went to Juxian to meet with Gao Guizi. Gao requested (1) to be reorganized under Ma Hongkui, (2) to first remove the besieging troops, (3) to provide appropriate back pay, and (4) that the Gao troops would depart for Tai'an within two weeks after the besieging troops were removed. The representatives did not dare to make a decision on these conditions on their own, so they came to Jinan to consult with Ma Hongkui and Chen Diaoyuan, and were accompanied by Gao's representative Han Shuzhi and Juxian's representative Wang Mingshuang. Representatives from Zhucheng and Juxian first met with Ma Hongkui, requesting that Gao's troops be reorganized under his command as soon as possible. Ma agreed. On the 14th, Chen Diaoyuan visited Ma Hongkui at the Jinan Hotel, where he happened to meet the representatives from Zhucheng, including Pei Mingyu. Pei and others reported the details of the negotiations to Chen and requested that the besieging troops be removed as soon as possible. Chen said that if Gao's troops were to be completely reorganized under Ma Hongkui, it might not be appropriate. The representatives said that when they negotiated with Gao Guizi, it was made clear that they would be reorganized under Ma's command. If there were any changes, Gao might not agree. They asked Chairman Chen to consider the people of Zhucheng and resolve the matter once and for all. Chen agreed to consult with Ma Hongkui. Chen was worried that Gao's troops might change their minds after the siege was lifted, but Ma Hongkui promised to take full responsibility and guarantee that Gao would not have other intentions. As a result, Chen agreed to let Ma take full responsibility for resolving the matter, but ordered Gao's troops to depart for Tai'an three days after the besieging troops were removed. Gao's troops requested to depart after two weeks. Regarding this point, Cao Jiqing, Ma Hongkui's representative, has gone to Juxian again to negotiate with Gao. After an agreement is reached, the besieging troops can be removed within a week. It is reported that there are 2,000 of Gao's troops in Juxian, 2,000 in Zhucheng, and 3,000 in Qingtuo Temple (100 li north of Yishui), for a total of over 7,000 people. According to the representatives, Juxian has not suffered other direct damage from the war except for commerce and food. Zhucheng, on the other hand, has suffered significant losses. Two-thirds of the houses in the city have been destroyed by bombing. In total, 40 120-pound bombs and 80 40-pound bombs were dropped by aircraft. One day last month, Fan's artillery fired over a thousand incendiary shells into the city, but were spared thanks to rain. Although the artillery fire was so intense, Gao's troops and the people were hiding in underground tunnels, so there were not many casualties. The Zhucheng war disaster is unprecedented in the past hundred years. The material losses are estimated to be over a hundred thousand yuan. (16th)

A Scene from the Vietnamese Independence Movement 68

▲Activities of the Vietnamese Nationalist Party

▲The Incident of February 10th

This year marks the centenary of France's occupation of Algeria. Celebrations are being held in Paris and its North African colonies, which are at their peak. France's overseas expansion has lasted for only a century. It initially developed in the Americas and North Africa, and then gradually planted its power in the Far East. After the Sino-French War in 1885, Annam became its protectorate. In 1898, it leased Guangzhou Bay. After the Great War, France regained a part of Germany's pre-war colonies. Thus, France became one of the largest colonial empires in the world, second only to Britain in terms of its vast overseas territories. At the London Conference, France demanded a large naval fleet, precisely to maintain communication between its motherland and its territories. At the same time, the government's plans and the parliament's proposals all focus on expanding overseas. Now that France has become a world colonial power, its newly emerging major industries and overly inflated financial capital must seek outlets overseas.

However, colonial powers cannot but rely on force as the foundation for their maintenance, and the peoples of various places, often fearing oppression, are prone to resistance. This year, India's independence movement has been relentless, and Gandhi's peaceful revolution is undermining the colonial policy of the British government. At the same time, the Vietnamese people, who have been silent for a long time, have also raised the banner of rebellion, and the French government cannot but pay attention to it. From this, it can be seen that the independence movements of the Eastern peoples, although temporarily quiet, have never ceased in secret.

The number of people participating in this Vietnamese Independence Party's rebellion was not large, and it was quelled in less than a day. Although the French government and the public are very calm, judging from the serious questions in the parliament and the various measures taken afterwards, it is not difficult to infer the seriousness of the internal situation. Although this incident arose in haste, its brewing was not a matter of a day. Since last year, the Annam national independence movement has gradually become active. Throughout last year, arrests of Annam political prisoners were frequently heard. Before that, the Annam nationalist movement had an organization called the Vietnamese Nationalist Party, which had been active secretly since last spring.

Most of the participants were young students and workers. At that time, its leader, Nguyen, was captured by the government and sentenced to three years of imprisonment. At the same time, 150 party members were arrested. In May and June last year, the French authorities searched various bookstores and newspaper editing agencies in Vietnam. Many students at the Vietnamese Normal School were also arrested due to the strike. On July 3, the Vietnamese Criminal Law Committee sentenced twenty-five Annamese to hard labor for fifteen, ten, and five years. Among those imprisoned were several women. On August 5, an Annam party member's entire family was arrested and imprisoned. On September 1, party member Nguyen Fangyan (?) committed suicide in prison. Although the government cracked down severely, the Vietnamese Nationalist Party continued its activities actively, and finally there was the bloody tragedy of February 10 this year.

The incident of February 10th was launched simultaneously in Yangbei (?), Honghe (?), and Hanoi (the above place names are transliterations of French names; I don't have a Chinese dictionary at hand to check, so I translated them according to the sound). The origin and course of the incident are still not clear. The following is based on the reports from the French authorities.

Yangbei, Honghe, and Hanoi are all in Tongking Province and are all important towns along the Kwong-Viet Railway. Hanoi is the capital of Tongking Province. Yangbei is only 200 li from the old border of our country and can reach Mengzi in a few hours. The Vietnamese Nationalist Party secretly mobilized soldiers stationed in Yangbei, who rose up at 1:00 AM and attacked the residences of French military officers, and occupied the armory. The French army was caught off guard and almost unable to resist. It was not until dawn that the French army began to gather the remnants and besiege the rebels. Before long, order was completely restored. More than twenty revolutionaries died, twenty-five were captured, and only three escaped. In addition, many Annam civilians were arrested. In this battle, five French military officers were killed and two were injured.

At the same time, in Honghe, more than twenty party members attacked the French military camp with pistols and bombs, but failed. They jumped into the Red River and fled, and many were captured by the French soldiers. Their leader died there.

On the evening of February 10, when the news of the Yangbei and Honghe revolts spread to Hanoi, the Hanoi party members seized the opportunity to respond. At that time, many party members riding bicycles threw bombs at the courthouse, the merchandise display hall, the police station, and the front of the French Governor-General's office, but no damage was caused. At that time, many people were captured by the French military police. According to those arrested, the purpose of throwing bombs was to prevent the Hanoi garrison from going to the aid of Yangbei.

The above is all information obtained from the French government. This incident arose suddenly, and only a few dozen people participated in the rebellion, so it was quickly quelled. By February 12, the entire Indochina was at peace. However, French troops are still searching for party members. Yesterday (March 28), the Vietnamese Criminal Committee (a special court established by the French government to try rebel criminals) announced the verdicts of those arrested in the Yangbei revolt. A total of thirty-nine people were sentenced to death, thirty-three were sentenced to life imprisonment, nine were sentenced to twenty years of hard labor, one was sentenced to five years of hard labor, and five were deported. According to investigations, five Frenchmen were killed before and after the incident, while more than thirty revolutionaries were killed in action, and thirty-nine were sentenced to death.

Because the incident occurred along the Kwong-Viet Railway and was very close to the border of our Guangdong, Guangxi, and Yunnan provinces, the French government suspected that the rebel party was instigated by communists from our country. We can certainly ignore this. In short, the Vietnamese people's independence movement is influenced by our country's National Revolution and India's anti-British movement, and its momentum is irresistible. It is feared that it cannot be stopped so easily. (March 29, sent from Paris by Lu Zi)

Wuhu Quick Dispatch 69

▲Bandit gangs in Fanchang County besieged the city. The commander of the Capital Garrison Regiment stationed in Wuhu, Lü Xueshu, recently personally led troops to suppress them. The Wuhu County Government also dispatched the Self-Defense General Regiment to assist, as ordered by the province. Yesterday, Lü's regiment encountered the bandits in Xinlinpu, near Fanchang, and engaged them in a fierce battle for several hours. The bandit leader Yang Laosi was killed on the spot, and more than thirty bandits were killed. Thirty-four long and short guns and several horses were seized. The remaining bandits scattered and fled, and are still being pursued. The Wuhu Self-Defense Regiment has advanced to Fanchang City, and the city has been turned from danger to safety. As for the bandit trouble in Guangde, Li Yuankai, the deputy commander of the Garrison Regiment, has also led the entire Third Battalion to suppress them. They arrived in Xuancheng yesterday, and along the way, they received several urgent telegrams from County Magistrate Zhou of Guangde, claiming that over eight hundred bandits had gathered at the border between Guangde and Changxing, threatening to attack Guangde, and the county seat was under extreme pressure. Li has now proceeded at full speed to discuss suppression methods with County Magistrate Zhou. The Garrison Regiment now only has two infantry companies remaining in Wuhu, led by Adjutant Huang Youyu. It is said that Huang will also lead troops to suppress bandit gangs that have emerged in Nanling County within the next few days.

The Wuhu Food Maintenance Association investigated the rice reserves in Wuhu and carried out registration. As a result, it was found that there were only over 30,000 shi of rice in the entire city, which is estimated to be enough for only half a month's food supply for the city. Therefore, inspections to prevent smuggling are even more stringent. People have also been sent to various rice mills and rice hullers to re-examine. If any excess rice is reported, it will be confiscated.

▲Due to the flood in the Baisha Embankment in Wuhu, the Provincial Relief Committee has allocated a relief fund of 1,000 yuan. The county government has now stipulated that it will be divided into three grades of four, five, and six yuan, and spring relief will be distributed on the 23rd. (16th)

Local Correspondence

Jiading 70

The Stadium Reverted to County Management: The Nanxiang Stadium was built by the former Township Administrative Bureau on land borrowed from the Zhende and Yuying Orphanages, with a subsidy of 1,500 yuan from the County Education Bureau. Recently, the Nanxiang Second District Office, which is in charge of management, found that the costs were too high and sent a letter to the Education Bureau requesting that it be reverted to county management. The Zhende and Yuying Orphanages have also agreed to the permanent loan of the 20 mu of land. Director Yang of the Education Bureau has reported the situation to the department for approval. Once a reply is received, it will be handled accordingly.

Arrest of Abductor Chen Er'a: A'xiao, the daughter of Wang Li of Malu, was lured and hidden in Shanghai by Chen Er'a last year. A lawsuit was filed with the county government. Recently, Chen Long, a detective from this county stationed in Shanghai, learned of the situation and requested the Shanghai court to arrest him. He was brought back for trial yesterday.

Page 12

Cranes in the Wind Amidst Bandit Alarms: The southwest of the eighth district of Jiading is mostly adjacent to Kunshan and Qingpu. Since the rampant bandits of the lake areas, residents have lived in a state of anxiety. The defense corps has been working overtime and patrolling, serving the public day and night. On the evening of the 16th, Jin Xiaodi, a farmer from Miaojing Village, went to a neighboring village for a celebratory banquet and saw people holding box cannons and pistols, walking eastward along the tracks. The number was quite large. He hid in fear, holding his breath for a long time. Another person, Mr. Jia, who was going to Zhangyan to comfort relatives who had been kidnapped, said that according to a ransom ticket who escaped from the bandit's lair, he learned that the bandits were coveting Anting. As a result, the city is filled with panic, and even the wealthy dare not live in peace.

Songjiang 71

Commemoration of the Founding of Nanjing as the Capital: The People's County Readjustment Committee convened schools, organizations, and groups at the County Party Headquarters auditorium today (the 18th) at 9:00 AM to commemorate the third anniversary of the National Government establishing Nanjing as its capital. Chairman Wang Tianren reported on (1) the process of establishing Nanjing as the capital, (2) the understanding we should have of establishing Nanjing as the capital, and (3) the efforts we should make in the future. Representatives Gan Yan, Cai Fucheng, Zhu Chengfu, and others then gave speeches. The meeting concluded with the shouting of slogans.

A Passenger from Jiaxing Dies of Poisoning: Yesterday (the 17th) afternoon, on the third or fourth class train from Hangzhou, a passenger who boarded in Jiaxing was bitten by a rabid dog. He was in great pain on the train. His ticket was for Songjiang Station. Upon arrival in Songjiang, he was spotted by military police, who ordered him off the train. He claimed to be a partner in a certain tea and food shop in Jiaxing, and had been bitten by a rabid dog. The poison had taken effect. The shop owner said he would send him home, but he himself was from Taizhou. It is unknown why the shop owner bought a ticket to Songjiang. He had no choice but to get off the train. As he spoke, his speech became increasingly slurred. After a while, he made sounds like a dog barking. The station staff sent him to the Second Precinct Police Station, who transferred him to a hospital. The hospital refused to admit him due to the severity of his condition, so they reported to the County Public Security Bureau for instructions. He died of exhaustion around 2:00 AM.

Suzhou 72

Large Gang of Lake Bandits Discovered in Xinkai Road: After the bandits on Yangcheng Lake were annihilated by the bandit suppression forces, the bandits who remained on Taihu Lake also reportedly fled to Zhejiang Province, temporarily disappearing. However, yesterday (the 18th) at around 11:00 AM, a group of bandits, about 300 in number, in over 30 boats, fled from Zhejiang Province to Xinkai Road, about ten miles from Wujiang. They were armed with sophisticated weapons, intending to harass the area. The leader of the 14th team of the Wujiang Water Police, Huai Zongbang, discovered this, and telegraphed Gong, the district chief of the 3rd district in Suzhou, for instructions. After receiving the telegram, District Chief Gong ordered the captain of the guerrilla force, Fang Yue, to instruct the leader of the 1st team, Ji Zongxian, to lead his team to intercept them. At the same time, he telegraphed Captain Huai to cooperate with the Wujiang garrison nearby to suppress the bandits. He also telegraphed the Bandit Suppression Headquarters to Commander-in-Chief Hu, who in turn instructed Zhao Xiguang, the Bandit Suppression Commander of the Eastern District, to immediately dispatch a team to suppress and arrest the bandits.

Murder Case Transferred to Suzhou for Trial: Zhou Peihua, a set painter at the Dongwu Theater in the Northern District of Suzhou City, was targeted by Ma Yao, who slaughtered chickens and ducks for a living last autumn. Ma Yao, wanting to seize Zhou's wife, lured Zhou to Nanjing, killed him with a chicken and duck knife, and abandoned his body in the wilderness. The case was discovered, and Ma was arrested. After repeated trials by the Jiangning District Court, Ma was sentenced to death. Ma was not satisfied and hired lawyer Bao Ying to appeal to the High Court. After approval, the Jiangning District Court yesterday transferred Ma to Suzhou for trial.

Three Bandits Arrested in a Robbery Case in Zhuangshang Village: On the 12th of this month, more than ten bandits broke into the house of Sun Xiangfu in Zhuangshang Village, Hengjing Township, Suzhou, and robbed him at gunpoint. They burned Sun's wife's lower body with a candle. As a result, several hundred silver dollars' worth of clothing and other items were stolen. On the 14th, the director of the 3rd Precinct, Jiang Tingxie, went to investigate. He soon learned that Du Youqing's house in Wushe Sanjia Village was harboring the robbers. He immediately arrested Du Youqing and a suspect named Ren Qingcheng, and recovered two original stolen copper items. According to Du Youqing's confession, the robbers were Shi Longsheng, who lived near Kongjiatang Bridge, etc. On the 17th, the precinct sent patrol officer Yao Shuwei to arrest Shi. Shi resisted arrest and threw rocks at the patrol officer, breaking his head. The patrol officer then fired two shots, hitting Shi's leg, and he was subdued and taken to the precinct. He confessed that he had colluded with Du Youqing and over ten bandits from other provinces to commit the robbery. Yesterday (the 18th), Shi, Du, and Ren were all sent to the County Public Security Bureau for trial.

Qingpu 73

The Li Family of Tiandu Beach Suffers Robbery: Li, a farmer from Qingpu's Tiandu Beach, in his forties, with a modest family fortune, was suddenly visited by over ten bandits carrying sharp blades around 10 PM the night before last. They broke down the door and barged into the bedroom. Li's family members had already gone to bed and were awakened from their dreams. They were immediately bound by the bandits, who then ransacked the house, stealing money, clothing, and other items before fleeing with their loot.

An Adulterous Affair of a Mother-in-Law Catching Her Daughter-in-Law: Ding, a farmer from Zhanggang Bridge in Qingpu's 9th District, had a wife, Gu, aged twenty-nine. They had been married for ten years and had a strong relationship. Yang, a bamboo craftsman in the same village, over forty years old and still unmarried, had an affair with Gu. The night before last, Yang was again having a secret rendezvous with Gu when her mother-in-law found out. She invited Xu, Mao, and two others to burst into the room and catch them in the act. The adulterer and adulteress were tied up together. The next morning, after persuasion from both sides' relatives and the village head, they were released. However, Gu Zhongwen, Gu's cousin, was not satisfied and reported to the 5th Precinct of Chonggu Public Security Bureau. After Yang, the precinct chief, received the report, he dispatched patrol officer Li and two police officers to arrest them. They immediately arrested Xu Mao and Wang Muying and took them to the precinct for questioning.

Fengxian 74

Execution of a Thief by Firing Squad: Ding Zhiyan, the captain of the county police force, cracked a major robbery case last month in Daoyuan South, on the 17th map of Jialu Li Zheng. The wanted criminal, Mei Jinxiang, and five others, were responsible for robbing Zhang Guisheng, a farmer from Tuolin Wai Zheng, the 17th map. They were sent to the judiciary for trial. They confessed to shooting and killing the victim. The stolen goods were recovered and verified. Except for the accomplices Wang Mulin, Wei Fuchang, and Wei Fulin, who were sentenced to life imprisonment according to the usual procedure, Mei Jinxiang was approved by the provincial authorities. Yesterday (the 15th), he was brought to court, identified, and escorted to the execution ground outside the South Gate of Fengcheng, where he was executed by firing squad as a warning to the public.

Personnel Change for Prison Warden: This county's prison warden, Lu, was dismissed after repeated prison breaks. The county submitted a request to the High Court. The vacant position has now been filled by Liu Ou, who passed the exam. He officially took office the day before yesterday.

Wuxi 75

A Communist Party Headquarters is Cracked: Zhu Zhengguo, the captain of the county police force, led police officers disguised as workers and arrested two key communist party criminals, Gu Yasi (also known as Gu Asi and Guan Lanting) and Xu Zhiliang, at the Daxing Foundry in Tongxian Road the day before yesterday. They seized various reactionary propaganda materials and took the landlord, Ni Alai, and his wife, Ni Baoshi, into custody for questioning. They learned that Gu Yasi had also set up a headquarters in a house at No. 21, Yizheng Road. Captain Zhu immediately led the detective team leader, Liao Dajin, and a squad of soldiers to investigate. They arrested Hua Xixian (nicknamed Mr. Li) on the spot and seized two suitcases of reactionary propaganda materials, including a central plan for riots and provincial and county plans. There were also two tightly sealed newspapers. Upon inspection, they turned out to be lists of Communist Party members. Captain Zhu then took the criminals and evidence to interrogate them. Yesterday, he transferred the five suspects, Gu Yasi, Hua Xixian, Xu Zhiliang, Ni Alai, and Ni Baoshi, along with the reactionary propaganda materials, to the county for trial. Zhou, the investigating judge, opened the court for interrogation. Gu and Hua confessed to being fake Communist Party committee members and that the Communist Party had set up a reactionary organization in Wuxi with three fake committee members, planning to launch a large-scale riot on May 1st. Xu Zhiliang confessed that he had joined the Communist Party in Shanghai last year through an introduction from someone and came to Wuxi to engage in propaganda work, having distributed leaflets once. Ni Alai and his wife, Ni Baoshi, claimed that they had rented a room to Gu Yasi and denied any knowledge of secret meetings or joining the Communist Party. After the interrogation, Gu Yasi, Hua Xixian, Xu Zhiliang, and Ni Alai were ordered to be shackled and imprisoned. Ni Baoshi was sent to the detention center for custody, pending further investigation.

Establishment of a Propaganda Committee: The Wuxi Propaganda Committee, after two meetings convened by the county's propaganda department with representatives from various agencies, has passed the organizational regulations. The county propaganda department was designated as the standing committee member, the finance bureau and the county government as the heads of the general affairs team, and the Jiangsu-Wuxi Journalist Association and the Sino-Western Women's School as the heads of the writing and speech teams, respectively. The expenses will be shared by various agencies, divided into two levels, A and B. Level A will contribute five yuan per month, and Level B will contribute three yuan per month. It was also decided that starting from April, each agency should immediately pay the funds to the finance bureau. The office location of the committee is temporarily set in the meeting room of the county party headquarters and will begin operations soon, with a report to be submitted to the provincial propaganda department for record.

Nantong 76

Joint Bandit Suppression Conference of Nine Counties in Jiangbei Held in Nantong: The provincial government commissioned Li Changjiang, the commander of the provincial police force, as the temporary bandit suppression commander for nine counties in Jiangbei: Nantong, Chongming, Haimen, Qidong, Taixian, Rugao, Taixing, Jingjiang, and Dongtai. Li established a headquarters in Nantong and scheduled a meeting on the 20th to discuss bandit suppression strategies with representatives from the nine counties. The local police force and militias are responsible for suppressing scattered small bandits within the borders.

Proportion of Regular and Additional Taxes to Land Price: The finance bureau received an order from the province to investigate and report on the proportion of regular and additional taxes to land value in the county. Cultivated land accounts for 9/1000. Reed fields and grassland account for 85/100,000. It is proposed to levy an agricultural improvement tax of two cents per mu, calculated at five jiao per liang, including the proportion of regular tax, cultivated, reed and grass land average to 52/10,000.

Naval Department Sends Gunboats to Suppress Bandits: Coastal areas of Nantong County are currently being harassed by sea bandits. The provincial government consulted with the Naval Department, which telegraphed the county government that shallow-water gunboats such as the Shun Sheng had been dispatched to suppress the bandits.

Reassignment of District Chiefs and Police Officers in Dongxiang: Due to banditry in various districts of Tongyi Dongxiang, the district chiefs and chiefs of the public security bureaus have all fled. The county government and the public security bureau have uniformly reassigned Li Zemao and others to take office. Because the lurking bandits have not been cleared, the bureaus in each district are temporarily merged into one office.

Yangzhou 77

Second Day of Strike by Educators Demanding Salaries: The education sector in this county has a large backlog of unpaid education funds. On the 15th of this month, Acting Director Gu originally intended to raise funds for half a month's salary, but because he was assigned to act temporarily, he was unwilling to take further responsibility. Therefore, all teachers and staff unanimously went on strike the day before yesterday, appealing to the education department to explain the difficulties and propose three conditions for resuming classes: (1) Before the colleagues resume their positions, the remaining half-month's salary for January and the full month's salary for February must be paid; (2) It must be guaranteed that at least the full month's salary for March will be paid before the traditional summer festival; (3) It must be guaranteed that after the March salary has been paid, the salaries for April, May, and June will be paid successively, with a maximum of one month's salary outstanding by the end of the semester. At the same time, the county magistrate was requested to urge the new director to take office quickly. Magistrate Chen replied that he had not received any notice of who the new director was and could not order him to take office based on a newspaper report. As for the remaining half-month's salary for January, the county government would raise the funds immediately.

Comfort Order from Provincial Department Head: Sun Hongzhe, the head of the Jiangsu Construction Department, issued an order yesterday to express his condolences to Wang Daoping, the head of the Jiangdu Construction Bureau, who was injured in a beating related to the Yanghuo Road project. He sent a doctor's diagnosis and the details of the treatment he had received in recent days, ordering him to rest and recuperate so that he could recover soon and continue to work hard.

Increased Competition Among Steamboats: Dada Inland Steamboat Company, due to current competition in the shipping industry, has advanced the departure time of its Yangzhou to Taixian route. Starting today (the 17th), it will depart every morning at 8:00 AM. It is also heard that various steamboat companies operating routes to Shaobo, Gaoyou, and other ports have a total of ten departures on odd days and twelve on even days.

Gaoyou 78

Investigation of Jail Warden Accused of Abuse: The county prison has deep-rooted abuses. Prisoners entering the prison are all required to "pave the way" (bribe), otherwise they will suffer various forms of torture. Several prisoners, because they could not bear the abuse of the jail warden, jointly filed a complaint with the High Court. The court has now appointed Judge Huang from Baoying County to investigate thoroughly. Huang arrived in Gaoyou last night and personally inquired about the situation of the prisoners in the prison this morning. In the afternoon, he returned to Baoying by car.

Bandits Rob Lujia Liu: At 4:00 PM the day before yesterday, two bandit boats suddenly arrived at Lujia Liu in this county. Seventeen bandits, each armed with a box gun, landed and robbed twelve families. The greatest loss was suffered by the family of Lu Yongzhong. It is said that the bandits dug up three cellars, with total losses estimated at about 10,000 to 20,000 yuan.

Rice from Shantaohe Rice Mill Held: Shantaohe Rice Mill is currently facing a shortage of rice in this county. The factory especially sent personnel to Shanghai to purchase 3,000 dan of Saigon rice to be transported back for relief. The rice was held back by the Shanghai Jianghai Customs. Now, the owner of the factory, Wang Mengshu, has specially discussed the matter with Chairman Chen of the Chamber of Commerce, who has sent a letter to Jianghai Customs. It is unknown whether the release of the rice will be possible.

Taizhou 79

County Government Appoints County Government Inspector: Hu Qingrong, the County Government Inspector of Linhai County, has submitted his resignation and has been approved. The vacant position has been filled by Lin Zheseng, who has already arrived and taken office.

Clans Gao and Xie Engage in Armed Clan Fighting: The Gao and Xie clans in Dianxi Village, Xixiang, Linhai, have recently started a conflict over trivial matters and have been engaging in armed clan fighting for days, with both sides suffering many injuries.

Two Bandit Leaders Killed in Licheng: Cheng Wenchai, Cheng Wengou, Cheng Wenxiang and others, bandit leaders in Licheng, Xixiang, Linhai, colluded with more than a thousand bandits and communists, burning and killing in the southwest of the county. The provincial government specially dispatched a large army to suppress them severely. The bandit leaders fled.

It is now known that the two bandit leaders Wen Gou and Wen Xiang were killed by their subordinates in Guankeng, Nanxiang. The heads were sent by the Nashan Security Corps of the same township to the county government and hung on the West Gate as a warning.

Jiaxing 80

County Government Holds Rice Conference: Jiaxing County Magistrate Jiang Zhicheng, concerned about soaring rice prices and the people's food supply, convened a Rice Price Stabilization Conference at the county government on the afternoon of the 17th, attended by various agencies and local figures. The following resolutions were passed: (1) Allocate 15,000 yuan from the rice price stabilization surcharge to cover the cost of handling rice price stabilization and purchasing Saigon rice for distribution; (2) The loss per stone will be set at two yuan; (3) A Rice Price Stabilization Committee will be formed; (4) The export of more than ten dan of rice outside the county will be prohibited until the new rice enters the market, in order to suppress rice prices.

Mobilization of Troop Reduction Bonds: Jiaxing County Government received a provincial telegram stating that the already-mobilized Troop Reduction Bonds should be collected and remitted as soon as possible, and that those not yet mobilized should be stopped. Therefore, County Magistrate Jiang has already remitted the mobilized Troop Reduction Bonds to the provincial department, and has ordered all personnel raising funds to stop raising funds.

Jiashan 81

Bandits Re-Kidnap Young Woman: Yang Mei, the daughter of the owner of a tofu shop in Yaozhuangqiao Town, was kidnapped by Xu Tianxiong's bandit gang when they went to Yaozhuangqiao to extort a large sum of money. She escaped during a fierce battle with the army and police. However, at about 3:00 AM on the 16th, the bandit gang led more than ten bandit boats with hundreds of bandits back to the town. Without looting, they re-kidnapped Yang Mei and headed towards Yuhui. The local gentry is now extremely alarmed.

Huzhou 82

Large Bandits Gather at Changqiao Checkpoint: The towns in the western part of Qing County have been harassed by bandits. Although they have been severely suppressed by the army and police, they have fled from one place to another. Recently, these bandits have joined forces with the Big Sword Society bandits who fled from Anhui Province. There are now more than 4,000 of them, concentrated at Changqiao Checkpoint, northwest of Lincheng Bridge and bordering Sian. The city of Lincheng and Sian are very tense. At 8:00 PM on the afternoon of the 14th, the 7th Company of the 2nd Regiment of the Security Force stationed in Lincheng immediately went to Sian to defend it, while the 9th Company set off to Changqiao Checkpoint to suppress the bandits. A telephone call was received from Lincheng Bridge, saying that at about 8:00 AM this morning, the army and bandits had opened fire on Changling, the road to Shangsian. Two companies of troops stationed in Huzhou set off this morning towards Sian.

Bandits Use Grave Digging as Threat: Shen's Yizhuang in the South Gate of the city, whose owner, Shen Tianxin, a local gentry, resides in Shanghai, is only occupied by a few caretakers. The day before yesterday, they suddenly received a letter from the bandits demanding 30,000 yuan, and stating that they had to meet at a certain place, with the messenger wearing mourning clothes. If they did not pay the money, they would dig up the ancestral tombs of the family on Bailong Mountain, and so on.

Hangzhou 83

Large Reef Discovered in Sanmen Bay: The Zhejiang Customs has announced that a large reef has recently been discovered between Dafuo Island and Yuandui Island in Sanmen Bay, at latitude 29 degrees 3 minutes and longitude 121 degrees 48 minutes 2 seconds. It has been verified to be a necessary passage for seagoing vessels and steamships. Yesterday, a notice was issued to avoid danger.

Changes Planned for City Public Security Bureau: The Zhejiang Provincial Department of Civil Affairs has approved the resignation of Mao Binglei, the director of the Ningbo City Public Security Bureau, who has repeatedly requested to resign. It is rumored that Liu Zuhan has been appointed to replace him. There are also rumors that Li Zizai, the director of the Hangzhou Public Security Bureau, will be transferred to another position, and that he will be succeeded by the current Haiyan County Magistrate Yan Youfu.

Pessimism About Silk Cocoon Market in Western Zhejiang: The silk cocoon market in western Zhejiang is closely related to the silk production of the entire province. However, due to the irregular cold and warm weather this year, many young silkworms have suffered from early diseases. In addition, due to bandit activity, many farmers have abandoned sericulture. In previous years, silk cocoon merchants would compete to seize land and occupy the market, but this year they are hesitant due to the bandits and difficulties in transportation. Therefore, the prospects for the silk cocoon market in western Zhejiang this year are not optimistic.

Xiaoshan 84

Abolition of Flower Tax Collection Office: The Zhejiang Department of Finance previously established temporary collection offices in Xiaoshan, Shaoxing, and other places to collect flower taxes when cotton was on the market. Now that the cotton season has passed, these flower tax bureaus are temporary in nature and are no longer needed. They have been abolished to save expenses.

Early Silkworms Entering First Sleep Stage: Early silkworms in Xiaoshan have begun to enter their first sleep stage. The weather has been alternating between cold and hot, causing many to die. Mulberry leaves are expected to be priced at five yuan per dan. Leaf merchants have scheduled scales to open in twenty-five or six days. There are not many sericulturists in the four rural areas this year, so the leaf market is likely to decline.

Ningbo 85

City Government Approves Village and Li Tax Measures: The Ningbo City Government held a municipal meeting yesterday and passed the following Village and Li Tax Measures: The Village and Li tax is based on households. The tax rate is divided into five levels: A, B, C, D, and E. The extremely poor are exempt. Level A households will be charged eight jiao per month, Level B four jiao, Level C two jiao, Level D one jiao, and Level E five fen. The level of each household will be investigated, reviewed, and registered by the Village and Li Committee and reported to the city government for verification and approval.

Public Cemetery Site Determined: The location of the Yongbo Municipal Cemetery was originally set at Dahe Bridge in Duan Tang. However, the area is too low-lying and unsuitable for building a cemetery. It is now known that the municipal health department has found a mulberry garden in Beibanhe that is suitable for use as a cemetery. However, the land area is only about three mu. Mayor Yang sent personnel to measure the land yesterday. If it is suitable, it will be transferred to municipal ownership and a cemetery will be built.

Settlement of Mob Damage to Public Security Bureau: The Public Security Bureau of Yokogawa-tou, Yuyao, was damaged by local people last month. The county government ordered that it be strictly dealt with. It is heard that the case has been actively mediated by local gentry. The houses, equipment, and missing firearms will all be rebuilt and compensated for by the people of the area, estimated at about 3,000 yuan. This has been approved by the county government.

Hefei 86

The Aftermath of the Dong Street Robbery and Murder Case: Since the Hengshunlong Money Shop on Dongmen Street was robbed and the owner, Li Shouzhong, was shot and killed, all shops in the city have been on guard. Da Yao Wan outside the East Gate, a vegetable stall owner, Guo Dafu, was robbed of 600 yuan the night before last and his son was kidnapped. The bandits demanded 1,200 yuan to be paid for his ransom at Jilugang in Shou County. Li Shouzhong's family also received a letter from the robbers yesterday, stating that they had not robbed them of 3,400 yuan and that their false report had damaged their reputation. They demanded that this amount be made up, or they would face severe consequences. All circles believe that the hidden bandits in the city are unscrupulous. A meeting was held at the Supplementary First Regiment Headquarters of the 45th Division, deciding that the Public Security Bureau, the Chamber of Commerce, and the Self-Defense Corps should jointly form an intelligence committee to investigate bandits. It was formed on the 12th to provide defense.
