Local News

Yesterday's Third Anniversary of the National Government Establishing its Capital in Nanjing 87

▲ Held a General Assembly at the Penglai Grand Theater

▲ Approximately 800 Representatives from All Sectors Attended

Yesterday was the third anniversary of the National Government establishing its capital in Nanjing. The Municipal Executive Committee held a Shanghai All-Circles Celebration of the National Government Establishing its Capital in Nanjing Commemoration and a Punish Yan Feng Two Rebels Propaganda Assembly at the Penglai Grand Theater on Penglai Road in the Southern City at 9:00 AM yesterday. Over 800 representatives from various institutions, groups, schools, and labor unions attended. Pan Gongzhan presided over the meeting, and Chen Guangyu from the Municipal Party Department and others delivered speeches. The Municipal Propaganda Department distributed various leaflets. Details are recorded separately below.

▲ Representatives Attending the Meeting: Pan Gongzhan, Bao Rong, Yang Qingyuan from the Municipal Party Department; Zhu Shujian, Wang Manyun, Guo Zhen, Gu Junjie from various district party departments; Feng Liutang, Yu Jianxing, Sheng Juncai from various bureaus of the Municipal Government; Wang Xuequan, Li Zheng, Chuan Depei from the Student Union; Liu Yunqian, Gu Yongquan from the General Labor Union; Lin Kecong, Xu Lanying from the Women's Association; Fan Baohua, Zhang Bin, Ren Suzhen, Xu Yuren from various schools; and Chen Jianzong, Xu Xingbai, Qian Siqian, Tong Baimei, Guo Shuliang, Wu Xianren, Shi Renzheng, Lu Shujie, Chen Weiyi, Cai Bubai, He Chengfu, Chen Ming, Pan Rongting, Chen Shusen, etc. from various branches, as well as all staff of the Municipal Party Department, totaling over 800 people.

▲ Assembly Staff: Chairman Pan Gongzhan, Recorders Wang Jinshan and Hu Yanyun, Master of Ceremonies Xu Yefu, Secretaries Hu Yuemei and Jiang Zhenwu, Receptionists Hu Xingyao and Zhang Tianbai.

▲ Assembly Order: (1) Music and Opening Ceremony (Municipal Public Security Bureau Military Band), (2) Sing the Party Song, (3) Pay the Highest Respect to the Party and National Flag and the Portrait of the Premier, (4) Chairman Reads the Premier's Will Respectfully, (5) Silence, (6) Chairman's Report, (7) Speeches, (8) Proposals, (9) Slogans, (10) Adjournment.

▲ Chairman's Report: Chairman Pan Gongzhan delivered the opening remarks, stating roughly: "Fellow comrades, today, representatives from all sectors of Shanghai have come here to hold a commemoration of the third anniversary of the National Government establishing its capital in Nanjing. At the same time, we must also list the reactionary behaviors of the current reactionary warlords, such as Yan Xishan, and arouse everyone's attention to jointly condemn them. Our commemoration of the National Government establishing its capital in Nanjing this time, especially in the current environment, when reactionary warlords and politicians are trying to establish a puppet government in Beiping, is particularly significant. We must encourage each other, consolidate the foundation of revolutionary forces, and strive to eliminate reactionary forces. Regarding the conspiracy to establish a puppet government in Beiping, we know that only Nanjing, historically, geographically, and culturally, is qualified to be the capital of the new China. The Premier's intention in designating Nanjing as the capital can be summarized in two points. First, Nanjing, from the perspective of Chinese history and culture, can very well represent the new vitality of China, can represent the spirit of the Chinese national revival, and can indicate the development of the Chinese revolutionary movement. Looking back in history, the national movements that occurred in Nanjing, not to mention the distant past, but just the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom decades ago, was the forerunner of the national revolution that our party is striving for. Although the actions of the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom were only narrow nationalism, they also had considerable reforms in economy and politics. Especially from the standpoint of nationalism, advocating the revival of the Chinese nation, we should pay attention to the fact that they took Nanjing as their political center. Furthermore, recalling five or six hundred years ago, when we were under the severe oppression of the Mongol rule, the success of the Han Chinese revival movement was also based in Nanjing. This history of national revival, often represented by Nanjing, cannot be erased, nor can anyone deny it. Why did Nanjing become the representative of the forces of national revival? There are reasons for this. Because the times and culture are advancing. During the period of struggle between new and old forces, one side represents the old forces, and the other represents the new forces. The center of the old forces is in Beiping, which was formerly Beijing, and the center of the new forces is in Nanjing. The reason why the Premier designated Nanjing as the capital was to encourage everyone to support the new doctrine and new forces to overthrow the outdated, evil, and feudal forces, so that the construction of the new China could proceed smoothly. Second, we should understand that since the end of the Qing Dynasty and the reign of the Beiyang warlords of Yuan Shikai's lineage, the failures of various international negotiations have created a supreme government above the Chinese warlord government, which is the so-called Legation Quarter in Dongjiaomin Lane, Beijing. Originally, the foreign affairs of a country, such as the issues between China and Japan, only need to be directly negotiated between China and Japan, and the issues between China and Britain only need to be directly negotiated between China and Britain. This is a certain principle. China is not like this. If you want to negotiate with one country, it is because the imperialists have organized a united front and used unequal treaties to bind us. Regarding China's problems, when China wants to negotiate with one country, they will definitely unite and form a joint force. The so-called Legation Quarter, the so-called Legation Quarter of various countries in the Boxer Protocol, has always been accustomed to holding the Chinese Beiping government hostage. We want to abolish the treaties, but they insist on revising the treaties. The Northern Warlord government, until its demise, did not even achieve a single point of treaty revision. Therefore, this is because they are afraid of the supreme government. If our government is still located in Beiping, under the control of these imperialist forces, this joint force cannot be broken. There is simply no new hope. Just look at Yan Xishan and others who want to establish a puppet government in Beiping, but first have to send people to Dongjiaomin Lane to get the Legation Quarter to smooth things over, and you can imagine that they have surrendered to the imperialists. Therefore, the National Government establishing its capital in Nanjing is the dawn of diplomacy. In the three years since the establishment of the Nanjing government, the diplomacy that has been conducted, even if there are places that cannot fully satisfy people, but from the perspective of not being coerced by the Legation Quarter, the first victory in diplomacy has already been achieved. From this perspective, the National Government's diplomatic actions have benefited from the establishment of the capital in Nanjing. Therefore, the Premier's designation of the capital in Nanjing is to break away from the control of imperialism. Domestically, we want to eliminate the decadent forces, the evil forces, and the feudal forces, to build a new China and develop the vitality of the nation. It is necessary to establish the capital in Nanjing. Externally, to break away from the coercion of the Legation Quarter, to break the shackles of imperialism, and to build a government of revolutionary diplomacy, it is also necessary to establish the capital in Nanjing. The Premier's designation of the capital, if scholars who study culture, history, and geography are asked to speak, they will definitely have many theories to support the Premier's proposal to designate Nanjing. Just from the above two points, we can already know how important the meaning of the Premier's designation of Nanjing as the capital is. It is indeed absolutely impermissible to violate it. If there are still people who advocate the establishment of a government in Beiping, no matter who is advocating it, they are undoubtedly reactionaries. That is, they do not want new development, they do not want the revival of the Chinese nation, and they are even the restoration of old ideas and old forces. Yan Xishan and Feng Yuxiang, as everyone knows, are feudal remnants of warlords, who only pay attention to their personal rights and territories. Now they are conspiring to organize a government in Beiping. We can only pity their stupidity. However, there are still many reorganizers and Western Hills Conference faction members who still talk about the Party and the Premier, who, for their own selfish interests, have taken refuge under the wings of warlords and want to establish a puppet government in Beiping. Can they still say that they are not counter-revolutionaries? Can they still not be condemned? This is the most important first point in today's commemoration. Second, let us think about why the National Government wants to move the capital to Nanjing. When the Party army recovered Hunan, Hubei, and Wuhan, and Nanjing had not yet fallen, the National Government had to move to the Yangtze River basin in order to coordinate political and military command. At that time, when politics and military affairs were developing, unfortunately, those Communists, who joined the Party in their individual capacity, wanted to usurp the Party and poison China. The Party had to deal with the warlords on the one hand, to implement the purification of the Party on the other hand, to save China on the one hand, and even more so to save the Party. Therefore, it implemented the purification of the Party and moved the capital to Nanjing. Therefore, firstly, we think that the National Government establishing its capital in Nanjing is still respecting the Premier's intention and has the significance of protecting the life of the Party and the vitality of the country. This is the first meaning of the commemoration. Today's commemoration is to be held once a year, and today is the third time. Why do we have this third commemoration? This is to allow us to review the work of the past three years to see if everything has been successful, which things have progressed quickly, which things have progressed slowly, and which things have not yet progressed. The Kuomintang's revolutionary movement is always forward-looking, but it does not mean that the platform of the Kuomintang's first national congress will be completed immediately after it is set. This is something that no one can do. Some people think that revolution should be like magic, changing in an instant. This is really a joke. With this illusion, they point out one or two points and create many shallow fallacies. As a result, people with weak wills are incited by them and unwittingly embark on the path of counter-revolution. Now, these reactionary elements, in addition to the warlords, are all inevitably based on this kind of erroneous idea. They do not know that with the vast land and large population of China, the completion of the revolution can only rely on the party's loyal leaders, inheriting the Premier's teachings, and leading the comrades of the whole party and the compatriots of the whole country, under the Three People's Principles, to first do the work of peaceful unification, stabilize and build China under the new forces, and take mutual trust and confidence as the foundation. Everyone recognizes that the purpose is correct, the motive is not mistaken, and they must enthusiastically do things and treat people with loyalty and forgiveness. We can use the Party's doctrine and platform as a measure to review past work. Today, we have advanced a few inches, and tomorrow, we have advanced a few feet. There is absolutely no reason to succeed overnight, and we must never scold, be indignant, be discouraged, or be romantic because we cannot see the emergence of a golden world. Young comrades should pay attention to cultivating their own physical and mental will. According to the Premier's will, encourage each other and do one part is one part. When we see doctrines and activities that are sufficient to endanger the survival of our nation and country, we must ruthlessly eliminate them. When we see rebellious elements that are sufficient to endanger the foundation of the Party and the country, we must support the Central Government to overthrow them. This is the attitude of comrades and this is the responsibility of citizens. This is the third meaning of today's commemoration. In short, firstly, moving the capital to Nanjing is based on the Premier's teachings; secondly, moving the capital to Nanjing is for the sake of saving the Party and saving the country; thirdly, commemorating the moving of the capital to Nanjing is to review the government's work with loyalty and forgiveness and to support the government's suppression of rebels. From this, we know that the actions of Yan Feng and the reorganizers, the Western Hills Conference faction, and other reactionary elements are completely against the Party, against the country, and against the Premier's teachings. They want to restore the old evil forces and are the sinners of the new China. Therefore, the representatives from all walks of life who attended the meeting today should tell this meaning to friends and relatives and let them all understand the wrongdoings of Yan Feng's rebellious behavior and the attitude we should take, only then can we truly commemorate the National Government establishing its capital in Nanjing. Next, Chen Guangyu from the Municipal Party Department gave a speech, details omitted.

▲ Assembly Proposals: There were two important proposals in the assembly: (1) To send a telegram supporting Chairman Chiang and eliminating the remaining warlords of Xiao Qing to complete the national revolution; (2) To send a telegram to the whole country to unanimously advocate suppressing Yan Feng. Both were unanimously passed by the assembly. The telegram was sent out on the same day. Details are as follows: (1) Telegram supporting Chairman Chiang and eliminating the remaining warlords of Xiao Qing, addressed to all newspapers, all levels of party departments throughout the country, all mass organizations, and overseas compatriots: "In recent years, the Party and the country have been unfortunate, and disasters have occurred frequently. Fortunately, thanks to the spirit of the Premier in heaven, the struggle of comrades, and the meritorious service of the soldiers, the Sun Wu warlords have been successively eliminated, and the Tang Zhang rebels have been exterminated, eliminating all corrupt elements. The people of the country are returning to the right path. The reactionary forces have been extinguished, and peaceful unification has been achieved. The political tutelage will begin from now on, the national revolution will be completed, recuperation will be carried out, and the country and the nation will be brought to a position of freedom and equality. How could it be known that Yan Xishan, who had received the grace of the Party and the country, dared to defy the great injustice of the world, advocating chaos, and holding the fallacious theory of propriety and concession as the state, coercing the Party and the country by having Chairman Chiang step down, secretly accepting the remnants of the shackles of the Anfu clique and the warlord rebels, and recruiting the Party and the country traitors of the reorganizers and the Western Hills Conference faction, regarding discipline as a mere formality, cruelly causing suffering to the people, regarding the Central Government as nothing, willingly becoming the head of the rebellion, and his reactionary behavior is extreme. Our Central Government is the Central Government for the welfare of the people, and our Chairman Chiang is the savior of the nation. Against this reactionary, we will now suppress him. To remove Qingfu is to make Lu safe. To destroy this feudal remnant is to complete the national revolution. At this time when the loyal and brave soldiers are working hard to kill the thieves in front, all the comrades and the entire people of this city are willing to uphold the revolutionary will of steadfastness and decisiveness and, together with all the comrades and compatriots of the whole country, unanimously support Chairman Chiang, quell this rebellion, and eliminate the remnants, and lay the foundation for peaceful unification forever. The national revolution will be completed. This telegram cannot express our extreme indignation." Shanghai All-Circles Celebration of the National Government Establishing its Capital in Nanjing Third Anniversary and Punish Yan Feng Two Rebels Propaganda Assembly. The Chinese Ratepayers' Association Issued a Declaration and Telegram Yesterday 88

▲ Foreign Minister Wang Also Issued a Declaration

The Shanghai Settlement Chinese Ratepayers' Association issued important documents as follows:

▲ Declaration to the Internal Public: "To All Citizens of the City, On the 16th of this month, the Western Ratepayers' Association overstepped its authority to discuss the proposal to increase the number of Chinese directors in the Municipal Council for this year, and McDonald, a British lawyer from the law firm of Cradock & Forbes (noting that this lawyer usually has the most Chinese clients), gave an arrogant speech. The Westerners present were incited by him, resulting in a rejection. All of us Chinese were deeply angered by this news. Our association convened an emergency meeting of representatives on the 17th and resolved to issue a formal declaration, confirming that the Western Ratepayers' Association has no right to discuss or decide on the civic rights that the Chinese ratepayers of the Public Settlement should have. Based on this principle, all rejections of the proposal to increase the number of Chinese directors by the Western Ratepayers' Association are naturally invalid. We have also publicly appointed Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, and Hu Mengjia as representatives to petition the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to negotiate based on reason to achieve our goal. The entire process has been witnessed. We must remember that Shanghai is the territory of the Republic of China. Foreigners rely on their imperialist power and use inappropriate methods to seize various inappropriate rights. We are fighting for the freedom and equality of the Chinese nation. Our greatest effort and ultimate goal is to recover the settlements. Before this goal is achieved, distributing the seats of the Municipal Council directors according to the proportion of settlement taxes is a fair and reasonable proposition. Previously, in order to avoid possible difficulties, we compromised and took the first step of adding three Chinese directors and then increasing it to five Chinese directors. Unexpectedly, the Western Ratepayers' Association overstepped its authority to discuss it, and Western ratepayers, such as McDonald, continued to follow their stubborn old mindset and wantonly attacked it, resulting in a rejection. We have suffered this great humiliation and should more deeply understand that only by the success of our ultimate goal can we obtain a firm guarantee and enjoyment of our Chinese civic rights. The responsibility for the subsequent destruction of the sincerity between Chinese and foreign citizens in the settlements should be borne by the Western Ratepayers' Association. The facts are clear and cannot be concealed. In addition to striving to quickly realize our fair and reasonable demands, our association also hopes that all Chinese citizens in Shanghai will have a deep understanding, make the greatest efforts, be of one heart and one mind, always remember this, and seek the ultimate success on the right track. Where justice lies, we will not look elsewhere. We hereby declare this to quell the indignation." Shanghai Settlement Chinese Ratepayers' Association Declaration, April 18, 1920 of the Republic of China.

▲ Telegram to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs: "To the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Nanjing, on the day the association selected the Chinese directors of the Shanghai Public Settlement Municipal Council, the matter was reported for filing. Unexpectedly, on the same day, the Western Ratepayers' Annual Meeting overstepped its authority to discuss the proposal to increase the number of Chinese directors in the Municipal Council by two, and the British lawyer McDonald gave an arrogant speech. The Westerners present were incited and blindly followed, resulting in a rejection. All Shanghai citizens were extremely indignant, and there was a tendency for swords to be drawn. In order to be cautious, the association convened an emergency meeting of representatives on the day after that and resolved to issue the following declaration: 'This association confirms that the Western ratepayers of the Shanghai Public Settlement have no right to discuss or decide on the civic rights that the Chinese ratepayers of the Public Settlement should have. Based on this principle, the rejection of the proposal to increase the number of Chinese directors of the Municipal Council by two by the Western Ratepayers' Association on April 16 of this year is naturally invalid. We hereby solemnly declare this.' We have also publicly appointed Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, and Hu Mengjia as three representatives to come to the Ministry to petition for a fair and just resolution in foreign affairs. In addition to comforting the citizens to listen to the Ministry's handling of the matter and unanimously vowing to be the backing, we respectfully request the Ministry to negotiate based on reason to achieve our goal and comfort the expectations of all Chinese citizens in Shanghai. Do not delay the anticipation of awaiting orders. Furthermore, the occurrence of this issue has caused a rupture in the sincere cooperation between Chinese and foreign citizens in the Shanghai Public Settlement, and the Western Ratepayers should bear full responsibility for this. We hereby solemnly declare this. We hope you will understand." Shanghai Settlement Chinese Ratepayers' Association. ▲ Letter to the Three Representatives: "Dear Sirs, Regarding the Western Ratepayers' Association's overstepping of its authority to discuss and reject the proposal to increase the number of Chinese directors at the emergency meeting of representatives of this association on the 17th of this month, it was resolved to issue a formal declaration based on the principle that the Western ratepayers of the Public Settlement have no right to discuss or decide on the civic rights that the Chinese ratepayers of the same area should have, considering it naturally invalid. Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, and Hu Mengjia have been publicly appointed as three representatives to go to Beijing to petition the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, negotiate based on reason, and achieve our goal. In addition to recording the case and sending a telegram to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and separate letters, we hereby send this letter for your information and implementation. Do not delay our anticipation. This letter is addressed to Representative Wang Xiaolai, Representative Yu Qiaqing, and Representative Hu Mengjia."

▲ The Departure Date of the Three Representatives: It is heard that Representatives Yu, Wang, and Hu have prepared their luggage and have telegraphed Foreign Minister Wang, saying, "To Foreign Minister Wang of the Nanjing Ministry of Foreign Affairs, we have petitioned the Ministry regarding the increase in the number of Chinese directors. Will you be in Beijing on the appointed day? Please reply by telegram, Yu Hede, Wang Xiao, and Hu Mengjia." As soon as they receive Foreign Minister Wang's reply, they will immediately rush to the capital. If Foreign Minister Wang comes to Shanghai in the near future, the three representatives will personally present everything in Shanghai, it is said.

▲ Letter to Manager Wang: "To Mr. Edwards, Consultant Phayre, General Manager of the Public Settlement Municipal Council, Dear Sir, This association formally issued the following declaration on April 17, 1920, of the Republic of China (as seen above). We hereby send this letter for your information."

▲ Assistance from the French Settlement: "Dear Sir, After reading the newspaper, we learned that the Western Ratepayers' Association of the Public Settlement overstepped its authority and resolved to cancel the proposal to increase the number of Chinese directors attending the Municipal Council. We cannot help but feel indignant. After reading your association's declaration, we find it to be righteous and dignified and worthy of admiration. We ask that you continue your past fighting spirit until your goal is achieved. Our association vows to do its best to assist. We hereby send this letter for your information." Shanghai French Settlement Chinese Ratepayers' Association, April 18.

▲ Foreign Minister Wang's Declaration: Regarding the Shanghai Public Settlement Ratepayers' Association's rejection of the increase in the number of Chinese directors, Foreign Minister Wang declared on the 18th: "The Shanghai Public Settlement Ratepayers' Association has now resolved not to allow the increase in the number of Chinese directors. I am truly shocked. The increase in the number of Chinese directors was previously agreed upon. Now, disregarding faith and righteousness, the stubborn foreigners have prevailed. This is truly regrettable. The recovery of the settlements depends on your leadership. I respectfully send this telegram to congratulate you, Fan Guang."

▲ Convening the Executive Committee: The association sent a letter to all executive committee members yesterday, "Dear Sirs, We have scheduled the first plenary meeting of this year's executive committee for 2:00 PM on April 19 in the reception room of the Shanghai Merchant Guild Readjustment Committee. In addition to sending separate letters, we hereby send this letter for your information. Please attend on time."

The Municipal Council Decides to Convene a Special Meeting 89

▲ New Trends in the Chinese Councilor Issue

Regarding the issue of Chinese Councilors in the Shanghai Municipal Council of the International Settlement and the unfolding of the stalemate, the Municipal Council, based on its position, has now decided to convene a special meeting of Western ratepayers to re-submit the proposal to increase the number of Chinese Councilors for another vote. The British Consul-General, Mr. Brenan, and the Japanese Consul-General, Mr. Shigemitsu, are currently

exerting all their efforts to bring this about, and some progress has been made. The information heard yesterday is compiled and recorded as follows:

▲ The British Consul-General Expresses: According to Mr. Brenan, the British Consul-General, he will use all his influence to push for the passage of this proposal at the special meeting. This meeting is convened in accordance with Clause 15 of the Land Regulations of the International Settlement. A petition with the signatures of twenty-five ratepayers will soon be submitted to the Municipal Council. Whether this petition has already been signed by twenty-five people is not yet known, as Mr. Brenan is not directly involved. However, he expects it can be completed. The definite news will be available within a day or two.

▲ Shigemitsu Agrees to Mediate: Japanese Consul-General Shigemitsu Kōki, in the interest of promoting Sino-Japanese amity, has also agreed to do his best to mediate. Although yesterday was a holiday, Mr. Shigemitsu still invited Councilors Fukushima and Saito, as well as several other Japanese community leaders, to his residence to discuss remedial measures. After the meeting, he also used

his personal capacity to invite consuls from various countries and members of various boards to discuss remedial measures for this case, and stated that he was willing to sincerely act as a mediator so that this case could be resolved satisfactorily as soon as possible, without causing resentment among Chinese and foreigners. It is now heard that next Tuesday (the 22nd), consuls from various countries and members of the Municipal Council will accept Consul Shigemitsu's invitation for an informal meeting to discuss solutions in the spirit of personal friendship. In addition, Councilors Fukushima and Saito are also working to mediate.

▲ Decision to Convene a Special Meeting: The Municipal Council believes that convening a special meeting of Western ratepayers in accordance with Article 15 of the Land Regulations of the Yangjingbang is the only way to remedy this issue and has now decided to convene it immediately. The procedures for convening the special meeting were generally described in yesterday's newspaper. If it does not fail to meet quorum, the issue has a good chance of being resolved. The detailed regulations for convening the special meeting are as follows: A special meeting of Western ratepayers may be convened temporarily to discuss matters if deemed necessary by all consuls or at the suggestion of at least twenty-five electors (i.e., ratepayers). The meeting must be held ten days after notification, and the agenda must be clearly stated in the notification in advance. A quorum of one-third of the electors is required. However, electors who cannot attend in person may send representatives. All resolutions must be passed by a majority to be valid. The meeting will be chaired by the senior consul, and if he is absent, a chairman will be elected by a majority vote of the electors.

Wang Xiaoda Rescued from Danger 91

▲ Kidnap Victim Hidden in Dapu Bridge

▲ Brave Rescue by Detectives

▲ Kidnappers Fled Empty-Handed

▲ Wang Xiaoda Safe and Sound

The case of Wang Xiaoda, the third son of Shanghai gentleman Wang Binyan, who was kidnapped, was successfully solved last night when he was safely rescued by the Shanghai Municipal Police Detective Squad. The details of the breakthrough are recorded as follows:

▲ After the Kidnapping: Since Wang Xiaoda was kidnapped by bandits on the 11th of this month at the intersection of Xinmin Road and Guoqing Road in Zhabei, there has been great concern from all sectors. The details at that time have been repeatedly reported in this newspaper and need not be repeated. However, since this case occurred, all sectors believe that if the son of the head of the local security organization, which is responsible for protecting local security, is kidnapped, one can imagine what might happen to others. Yuan Liang, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, paid special attention to this and issued an order to his subordinates to solve the case in the shortest possible time.

▲ Location of the Bandits' Den: After Director Yuan issued the order, he especially summoned Lu Ying, the acting head of the Detective Squad, to encourage him to intensify the investigation. After receiving the order, Director Lu immediately ordered his subordinates to conduct a thorough investigation. Several days passed with no news. Unexpectedly, the night before last (the 17th), a confidential report stated that the bandits' den was located in a bungalow at No. 10 Chengzhili, Tanjiazhai, in the far western Chinese territory of Xujiahui. However, it was not certain whether the kidnap victim was inside. He was asked to quickly send officers to arrest the suspects. After receiving the report, Director Lu immediately assembled more than twenty officers, personally led them, equipped with weapons, and first went to the Second Precinct of the Sixth District to meet with the chief police officer. They rushed there at night. ▲ Where the Kidnap Victim Was Hidden: When they arrived at Tanjiazhai, it was not yet dawn, and they could not distinguish east from west. Director Lu then led the officers to crawl through the nearby wilderness and fields, waiting for dawn. When the east turned slightly white, he ordered the house to be surrounded first, and he took the lead in rushing in. However, the house was empty, with no one inside. After a detailed inspection, many clues were found, indicating that the bandits had three hideouts and had already moved elsewhere. He then led the officers back to the team and intensified the investigation. It was then discovered in the afternoon (yesterday) that the location where the kidnap victim was hidden was in a house at No. 5 Yongdeli, Dapu Bridge West, Xujiahui Road, within the French Concession. At about 6:00 p.m. that evening, Director Lu personally led detectives Qi Haitian, Han Ruisheng, Zhang Guangsen, Wang Peiwen, Ding Shunqi, Zhou Peisan, He Haifa, Shan Bin, Han Jingxiang, Hou Shenghan, Zhang Yingpin, etc., to make the arrest.

▲ Like Obtaining a Treasure: Director Lu led the officers in several cars and first reported to the special agency of the French Police. At the same time, he ordered Detective Ding Shunbao to first rush to check on the house at No. 5 to facilitate an immediate rush in to avoid searching for it at the last minute. When they arrived at Yongdeli, they saw a single-story Shikumen house at No. 5. However, the upstairs and downstairs were dimly lit. At the same time, Director Lu and Chinese and Western detectives from the French Police arrived one after another. They rushed in together, directly rushing upstairs. The house was empty. When they searched the room on the overhead bridge on the second floor, they caught a glimpse of a person wearing a black short jacket lying on a couch, with a lamp dimly lit on the wall. The detectives went forward and pressed him down. Upon closer inspection, it was none other than the kidnap victim Wang Xiaoda. The detectives were as if they had obtained a treasure.

▲ Danger of Being Killed: After Director Lu rescued the kidnap victim, he ordered a search of the entire house, but it was empty. When he asked the kidnap victim, he said that he had heard the news and fled. He first brought the kidnap victim into the police station and asked him a few questions. Then Director Lu personally led the team and immediately notified the family by telephone. His father, Wang Binyan, rushed over upon hearing the news and deeply thanked the detectives for their effective rescue. According to Wang Xiaoda, he was taken directly to that place after being kidnapped and was initially hidden in the attic, where he ate very coarse food. He was only moved to the overhead bridge room yesterday morning. So far, he has not been mistreated. There were eight or nine people guarding him, taking turns. The bandit leader spoke with a Jiangbei accent, wore a Zhigong woolen mandarin jacket and a woolen hat, and was neatly dressed, looking like a businessman. As of yesterday morning, the bandits suddenly gathered to discuss privately, saying that if there were no results today (yesterday), they would definitely kill him that night. After finishing, he was personally led back by his father. Director Yuan was very pleased to hear the news and planned to reward the officers who contributed, depending on their merits.

Public Concession Intensifies Precautions Against Western Shanghai 92

▲ Armed Police Search Pedestrians

▲ Trams and Cars Also Not Exempt

The Chief Inspector of the Shanghai Municipal Police in the Public Concession, due to the recent frequent occurrences of robberies and kidnappings in various places, especially in the western Shanghai area, where workers are mixed and of mixed quality, has ordered the Jing'an Temple and Gordon Road police stations to strengthen precautions. Yesterday afternoon, at about 5:00 p.m., the Jing'an Temple police station dispatched a Western police officer, leading two Japanese police officers and six Chinese police officers, all wearing iron vests and carrying live ammunition pistols, to go to Jessfield Road, Brenan Road, Yu Yuen Road, etc., to conduct random searches. All pedestrians, vehicles, public buses and trams were required to temporarily stop for a thorough search. The security measures were extremely strict and only withdrawn in the evening.

A Haggard Young Man Dies Tragically in the Oriental Hotel 93

▲ Checks into Hotel Alone ▲ Looks Like an Ill Person

▲ Suddenly Takes Poison Late at Night ▲ Cause Not Understood

The Oriental Hotel at the intersection of Hankou Road and Zhejiang Road received a guest around 7:00 p.m. the day before yesterday. He was wearing a dark blue serge jacket, black serge trousers, white socks, and gabardine shoes. He registered as Chen Zhenchu, 24 years old, from Hangzhou, and worked in the Western medicine business. He stayed in room 104 on the ground floor of the hotel and did not have a meal. He looked haggard, rather like someone newly recovered from a long illness, and the tea room did not pay much attention to him. After Chen Zhenchu closed the door, he stayed inside for a long time. Around midnight, he rang the bell to consult the tea room, saying, "I have something to do tomorrow and need to be woken up at 9:00 a.m." The tea room attendant replied politely, and Chen closed the door and went to sleep. Unexpectedly, at 9:00 a.m. yesterday, the attendant went to room 104 to call him as agreed and called out loudly at the door. After several calls, there was no response, presumably because he was sleeping soundly. He knocked on the door, making a loud noise, but there was still no movement. Feeling suspicious, he reported to the accounts room. The manager, upon hearing the news, thought that there had been many suicides in hotels recently, and this gentleman was probably no exception. He urgently ordered the door to be pried open. They saw Chen Zhenchu lying stiffly on the bed, his eyes rolled back, his mouth open, and his hands and feet still slightly moving. They also saw an empty bottle of sedative medicine on the table, a piece of cigarette paper, and a little sorghum wine. The tea room attendants knew that he had taken poison. They immediately reported to the Old Gate police station. The police chief immediately ordered Chinese and Western detectives to investigate. When they arrived at the hotel, they saw that Chen was already dying. They searched his body but found nothing of value. He was sent to Renji Hospital for treatment. After examination by the doctor, it was determined that he had taken too much poison and could not be saved. He died shortly afterward. It was decided to send him to the forensic examination center on Faelan Road this morning for an autopsy.

Luo Qingfen Accuses Zhang Wenzheng of Bigamy 94

▲ Sweet Words at the Time of Engagement

▲ Landed Property, Never Had a Wife

▲ After Marriage, Came to Shanghai, Treated Like a Stranger

▲ Only After an Investigation Did She Realize She Was Deceived

Zhang Wenzheng (also known as Zhang Yunqing) from Nanxiang, formerly married Luo Qingfen as his wife, is now being sued by Luo through lawyer Wang Shizong for bigamy. The court hearing took place at the Special District Local Court. Judge Wu presided over the hearing the day before yesterday. The defendant, Zhang Wenzheng, did not appear. According to Luo's claim, she is 26 years old and originally from Shaoxing. She married Zhang on the 21st day of the first month of last year. The matchmaker was Wang Abao. After marriage, they lived together in Huashunli, Tongfu Road. At the time of the engagement, the defendant claimed that he was a compradore in Ander Yiyang, had landed property, and had never had a wife. Therefore, in the third month after the marriage, she accompanied him back to the old house in Hualiu Stone, Nanxiang, stayed for about a week, and then came back to Shanghai. Then the defendant suddenly stopped coming to my house and did not provide support. Last December, I gave birth to a son. I informed the defendant, but he ignored it, treating me like a stranger. Later, after investigation, I learned that the defendant had a wife at No. 1112 Xinpingli, Yanlongmen Road. The defendant has committed bigamy and I request punishment. Then the officer who served the subpoena reported that he went to Xinpingli to summon the defendant. The second landlord of the house said that there was a tenant named Zhang, but he was not named Wenzheng or Yunqing, so he could not be served. Judge Wu adjourned the case, instructing the plaintiff to cooperate with the bailiff to summon the defendant to court for further investigation.

One Word Causes Death 95

▲ Female Worker Is Competitive

▲ Provoked by a Coppersmith's Words

▲ Installing a Belt on a Motor

▲ A Tragedy Occurs

Shen Sigen from Shenjiazhai, west of Xinjing Town in northwestern Shanghai, married Du Xiamao's sister, Xinying (i.e., Shen Du, 25 years old), who ran a steamed bun shop in Beixinjing, three years ago. She had been a female worker in the cloth machine room of Toyota Textile Mill in Zhoujiaqiao for eight years. On the afternoon of the 16th, at 4:30 p.m., Xinying was working in the factory when the belt suddenly fell off. A coppersmith in the same room jokingly said to Xinying, "If you can install the belt on the motor, I will admire you." Xinying, in a moment of competitiveness, installed the belt on the motor. Unexpectedly, at that time, the wheel was spinning very fast, and it caught Xinying's hair. In an instant, her whole body was lifted up. By the time she was rescued,

both of her hands were broken, and her neck and chest were severely injured, with blood and flesh blurred, a truly tragic sight. She was rushed to the Red Cross Hospital on Haig Road for treatment, but her injuries were too severe, and she died at 7:00 p.m. that evening. Because the weather is getting hotter, the family first collected the body and is asking the factory for compensation and severely punishing the coppersmith while reporting to the local Party branch and Municipal Councilor Chen Ya-fu, requesting assistance.

First Day of the Wusong Fishing Season 96

▲ One Fishing Boat Arrived Yesterday Afternoon

▲ Three and a Half Holds of Fish Sold Out in Half a Day

The annual Wusong spring fish (commonly known as Northern Yellow Croaker) fishing season, and the fishing boat of Chen Heshun, manager of the Cuisheng Fish Shop on Gui Zi Road, arrived in Wusong first from outside the port at about 3:00 p.m. yesterday (the 18th), fully loaded with three large holds of spring fish. After the Wusong Changguan customs officer of the Jianghai Customs went to inspect the boat, the Cuisheng Fish Shop immediately set off firecrackers and hung red banners to start the weighing process as usual. The price was twelve catties per scale (i.e., twelve catties of spring fish sold for one yuan, according to last year's opening price of fourteen catties per scale). After receiving the news, general fish merchants from the surrounding areas rushed to Cuisheng to buy fish and transport them to various places for sale. By about 7:00 p.m. yesterday, the entire boat of fish had been sold out. According to Chen Heshun's boat crew, there are still many fishing boats behind them, and they will also arrive at Songbu last night or this morning.

Christians Held Mass Yesterday 97

Yesterday (the 18th) was the day of the Catholic Good Friday (commonly called Foreign Qingming). Both the Dongjiadu Catholic Church in the Nanshi and the Yong'an Street Catholic Church in the French Concession held the Mass of the Passion of Jesus starting at 7:00 a.m. Celebrations lasted until 10:00 a.m. At 3:00 p.m., ceremonies such as the Sacred Good Works and the Stations of the Cross were held. Chinese and foreign male and female believers in the church attended the service, recited scriptures, observed the ceremony, and listened to the priest's lecture on the beginning and end of Jesus' Passion until 4:00 p.m. Tomorrow (the 20th) is the Great Feast of the Resurrection of Jesus. Zhang, the church manager of Dongjiadu Catholic Church, and Neng, the director of Yong'an Street Catholic Church in the French Concession, ordered the workers to hang colorful silk banners inside and outside the church. Yao, the bishop of Jiangsu Province, will hold the Great Mass of the Resurrection of Jesus at 8:00 a.m., chanting scriptures and playing music. At 2:00 p.m., there will be a blessing with the Holy Body. It will be a grand occasion.

Police Officer Colludes with Former Inspector to Defraud Money 98

▲ On the Pretense of Introducing Business

▲ Defrauding Small Workers of 900 Yuan

Wu Guisheng, a Chinese police officer No. 416 of the French Police, colluded with Yao Shousong, a former inspector of the Great World, last month, and used fraudulent means, on the pretext of recommending business, to defraud Yu Caikang, Jiang Hongliang, Hou Gaohui, Qi Fenggui, Tang Luchang, Chen Wanshan, Ma Zhengyuan, Ma Deyuan, and other eighteen people of 900 yuan in silver dollars. Later, Yu and others discovered the fraud and reported it to the French Police, who ordered detectives to arrest Yao alone. Wu Guisheng, the police officer No. 416, had already fled upon hearing the news. The police station sent Yao to the French Public Court for investigation the day before yesterday. The plaintiffs Yu Caikang and others all stated that they had always made a living doing odd jobs. Previously, police officer No. 416 said to them that the Great World was recruiting staff, and

he could ask Yao Shousong to help them get in. They believed it to be true and each paid 50 yuan, gathering over 900 yuan and inviting Yao Shousong to a feast at the Sanhe Lou restaurant. The plaintiffs handed over the money to police officer No. 416, who then handed it over to Yao Shousong. Unexpectedly, the defendants repeatedly delayed and disappeared. Therefore, they were forced to report to the police station and arrest Yao. The money of the plaintiffs was all borrowed from others. They requested a strict investigation. When Yao Shousong was questioned, his lawyer defended him, saying that although the defendant was present at the feast, he did not mention the matter of recommending business, nor did he receive the money from No. 416. He was falsely accused and requested a clear investigation. The Chinese and Western officials ordered Yao to pay 400 yuan for bail and be released, pending further investigation.

Telegram on Defeating Lake Bandits in Si'an 100

▲ Recapture of Si'an at Noon

▲ Pursuing Remaining Bandits

The Songhu Garrison Headquarters received telegrams from Huzhou and Suzhou yesterday, recorded as follows: (1) Chief Commander Hu telegraphed from Huzhou on the 18th, stating: (1) I arrived in Wuxing last night. The Si'an bandits were jointly suppressed by the Zhong and Hang regiments, killing more than 200 bandits. They are now fleeing towards Meixi, and our troops are in pursuit. (2) More than 1,000 bandits gathered near Meishan Huangyuanli in Wuxing. I have dispatched troops to suppress them and expect to eliminate them soon. (2) The Suzhou Bandit Suppression Headquarters forwarded a telegram from Commander Zhong on the hour of 酉 (5-7 PM), stating that bandit leader Zhang Minggao led more than 1,000 men to capture Si'an in the morning. On the hour of 辛 (3-5 PM), the Hang regiment assisted my troops, engaged in a fierce battle with the bandits near Kongshan for five hours. At noon, Si'an was recaptured. The bandit regimental commander Wang, a bandit lieutenant colonel regimental adjutant, a knife guard training instructor surnamed Yu, and more than 300 bandit soldiers were killed on the spot. More than ten wooden-cased guns, rifles, countless sabers were seized, and more than 100 remnant bandits were captured and scattered, with many fleeing south. They are currently being pursued.

Sino-French Vietnam Agreement Difficult to Sign Temporarily 101

▲ French Minister Maraud to Take Post as Ambassador to Japan Next Month

The Sino-French Vietnam Trade Agreement, which has been stalled for a long time, was rumored last week to have hopes of being signed soon. It was said that because the French Minister Maraud saw that our Commissioner Zhang Weihan was about to return to Guangdong, he specifically sent a note to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs

expressing his sincerity in signing the agreement, but he did not specify the date of his southward journey. According to news from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs yesterday, there is absolutely no hope of signing the trade agreement in the near future. The French Minister knows that our side will find it difficult to accept the conditions he has attached, so he is being mysterious and using it as an excuse to delay. It is also heard that the French Minister has decided to leave for Japan in early May to take up his post as ambassador. Therefore, the signing of a new agreement between the two sides will have to wait until the new French Minister Verdun arrives before negotiations can be held.

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce telegraphed Suzhou Provincial Government yesterday to support the Suzhou Provincial Government's reduction of administrative expenses of various agencies, and requested the abolition of various petty miscellaneous taxes within the scope. The telegram stated: "Zhenjiang Provincial Government, having read the report that the Second Eighty-Fourth meeting of your government resolved to reduce the expenses of various agencies, divided into six items, a total reduction in monthly expenditure of 115,801 yuan, an annual reduction in expenditure of 1,389,612 yuan. The thrifty movement should start from above, and the provincial government has reduced its expenses even more, in line with the principle of setting an example. Since the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, the financial resources of the southeast have supported the overall situation, but the resources have been exhausted. In addition, the disasters and famines of recent years, and the rampant lake bandits, have spread throughout the villages and towns, and farmers and merchants are struggling. The orders and proclamations are praised, and the people are hopeful. We hope that your government will have the determination to clarify the situation and abolish petty miscellaneous taxes within the scope of provincial taxes, so that even thatched huts can benefit, and with sufficient food and clothing, the sources of chaos will be suppressed. This is the first key to governing the country today. In addition to our gratitude and comfort, we offer our humble opinion, hoping that you will not abandon it and adopt it. We would be greatly honored. The Shanghai Special Municipality Businessmen's Organization Rectification Committee bows and salutes."

The Urgency of County Police Demanding Military Pay 106

▲ Magistrate Leng Promises to Allocate 2,000 Yuan

The branch directors of the Shanghai County Public Security Bureau, because the police pay has been in arrears for more than three months, the food of the police officers has been cut off, and they are clamoring every day. The stores are demanding the payment of debts, so they are unable to maintain it. Yesterday, they gathered in the city and appealed to the head office to demand payment. Shen Zhenhua, the director of the bureau, had no choice but to go to the County Government with them at noon to see Magistrate Leng. Yesterday also happened to be the anniversary of the establishment of the capital, and the office was closed. Therefore, they went to Magistrate Leng's residence in the French Concession to present the situation in person and demand a real remedy. As a result, Leng ordered the Finance Bureau to allocate 2,000 yuan of the financial aid from the Department of Finance in advance for distribution to maintain the current situation temporarily, and then discuss a fundamental solution. The branch directors then left and returned to their bureaus.

Record of the Japanese Chamber of Commerce General Meeting 109

▲ Hopes for Development in Sino-Japanese Trade

The Continental News reports that the Japanese Chamber of Commerce in Shanghai held its general meeting at the Japanese Club last night (the 17th). Thirty-two leading figures from the business community attended. Chairman Mr. Miri reported on the Chamber's work over the past year and the political and commercial situation in China. He stated that although the situation in China was still unstable last year, the total foreign trade reached 242.5 million taels, an increase of 23.9 million taels compared to 1928 and 49.5 million taels compared to 1927. However, the total Sino-Japanese trade volume was only 90.09 million Japanese yen.

, a decrease of 16 million Japanese yen compared to 1928. Furthermore, last year's total value of Chinese imports was 129.8 million taels, and the total value of exports was 112.7 million taels (i.e., an import surplus of 17.1 million taels). The total value of imports from Japan was 53.2 million Japanese yen, and exports were 37.7 million Japanese yen. (Translator's note: Last year's trade deficit with Japan was 15.5 million Japanese yen, equivalent to about 12.3 million silver taels, accounting for more than one-third of the total foreign trade deficit. The value of imports from Japan accounted for about one-third of the total foreign imports, while the value of exports accounted for more than one-quarter of the total exports.) The Sino-Japanese tariff agreement is expected to be approved soon, and the issue of consular jurisdiction is also expected to be resolved peacefully shortly. The gradual restoration of Sino-Japanese diplomatic relations should greatly contribute to the development of trade between the two countries, etc. Subsequently, new officers were elected and the meeting adjourned. As a result, Mr. Miri (Nissin Company) was re-elected as chairman, and Mr. Sakurakawa (Mitsubishi Company) was elected as vice-chairman.

Ministerial Order: Old Company Regulations Still Temporarily Applicable 110

The Commercial Reorganization Committee sent a letter to the Chromolithography Trade Association, stating: Previously, a letter was received asking whether to apply the old regulations or the new law since the Company Law's implementation date has not been determined, and requested instructions from the ministry for compliance. After reporting the situation via telegram, a return telegram was received from the Acting Minister of Industry and Commerce on the 12th of this month, stating, "The telegram has been received. The implementation date of the Company Law was previously submitted to the Executive Yuan, which approved the Legislative Yuan's reply. The implementation date of the Company Law should be specified in the implementation rules." A ministry order has been issued regarding this matter. Before the promulgation of these implementation rules, all matters concerning companies shall still be subject to the old company regulations. This information is to be relayed to the Association and circulated for knowledge. Therefore, this letter is specially prepared to inform you, and it is hoped that you will take note."

Commodity Inspection Bureau Dispatches Personnel to Zhejiang to Investigate Tung Oil Conditions 111

In addition to the chemical testing work of various inspection departments within the bureau, the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau's Chemical Testing Department also pays attention to researching the improvement of commodities. The bureau considers tung oil to be a special product of China, with a large quantity being shipped overseas each year. To maintain the credibility of the international market and develop foreign trade, it is necessary to vigorously seek improvement. Therefore, it has specially dispatched technician Shou Le from the Chemical Testing Department to Jinhua, Lanxi, Quzhou, Wenzhou, and other places in Zhejiang to investigate the production conditions and oil extraction methods of tung oil. In addition, official letters were sent to the magistrates of each county, requesting assistance, protection, and various conveniences after the personnel arrive.

Posthumous Honor for Zhang Rutong 112

▲ Died from Gunshot Wounds While Bravely Capturing Thieves

▲ Municipal Government Public Safety Bureau Awards Plaque

On March 2nd of this year at 8:15 PM, Ren Ruqi's family at No. 1 Dongshengli, Tangjiawan, in this city, was targeted for robbery and kidnapping. Zhang Rutong, a nearby resident, heard the commotion outside and mistakenly thought it was a fire. He went out to investigate, discovered it was a robbery, bravely pursued the thieves relentlessly, and was shot and killed by the thieves. As a result, the kidnapped young child of the Ren family was abandoned and safely rescued. The Municipal Public Safety Bureau, recognizing the deceased's profound sense of neighborly concern and selfless rescue efforts, commendable and respectable bravery, awarded a plaque inscribed with the four characters "Martyr for Justice, Forgetting Self," and raised one hundred yuan for consolation. It also obtained approval from the Municipal Government to award a plaque inscribed with the four characters "Commendable Righteous Courage" to serve as an example and promote awareness.

Foreign Press Commentary on China's Postal Service 113

The English "Financial and Commercial News" of March 19th of this year commented on China's postal service. Excerpts are translated below for reference. On March 15th of this year, the new organization specializing in postal financial affairs (Postal Savings and Remittances General Bureau) held its opening ceremony presided over by the Minister of Communications. Thus, the postal savings and remittance business is formally separated from ordinary postal delivery services. This reform follows the established practices of development policies in various countries and is expected to benefit all parties. This approach allows the original Post Office General Bureau to focus on postal matters, while simultaneously establishing the Postal Savings and Remittances General Bureau to promote savings and enable the public to save small amounts of money through this new institution. Most notably, on the opening day of the Postal Savings and Remittances General Bureau, over one thousand new accounts were opened under the name of the new bureau. This is truly a good omen. It is heard that the General Bureau has over two thousand one hundred and twenty-five branches located throughout the country. In discussing postal matters, one is reminded of a clearly visible source of income mentioned in this newspaper before, which is substantial and does not cause significant harm to individuals or groups. However, the Chinese government has apparently not paid attention to it, namely that China's postal rates are too low. Currently, the postage for a local letter within China is only one silver cent, which, based on the current silver price, is only equivalent to 0.00175 of a penny. The postage for a letter sent to any location within China thousands of miles away is only four silver cents, less than three farthings. These rates are far lower than those of other countries and could be slightly increased. This would not hinder anyone and would greatly benefit government revenue. If the Chinese authorities adopt and implement this suggestion, we will inevitably be criticized by those less virtuous than ourselves. However, we know that this proposal is honest and selfless, and we can use this as an argument against criticism. Furthermore, it should be noted that our proposal is only to slightly increase postal rates.

Consolidation and Reorganization of Rice Industry Organizations 115

▲ Reply from the Municipal Government to the Municipal Party Headquarters

The Municipal Government replied to the Municipal Party Headquarters yesterday, stating: "Previously, we received a letter from your association regarding five resolutions of the Municipal Government submitted by the Sixth District Party Headquarters, concerning the Fourth District Representative Assembly, requesting review and reply. The relevant bureaus were instructed to review and reply, and a response was sent to your association. Now, according to the Social Affairs Bureau's report, we have copied and issued the original case of unifying rice industry organizations, instructing investigation and reporting. Upon investigation, we find that regarding item (A) of the original resolution, concerning the abolition of organizations of brokers, factories, shops, and sales agents, and the formation of a 'Grain Industry Association,' the Municipal Commercial Organization Reorganization Committee has already been separately merging and reorganizing them in accordance with the provisions of the Industrial and Commercial Trade Association Law. Once the reorganization is completed, unification will be achieved naturally. Regarding item (B), concerning the abolition of the dou and hu measurement system and the universal adoption of weight measurement, the rice industry's import and export have traditionally used the dou and hu system due to custom, which naturally has its drawbacks. However, forcibly changing to weight measurement at once is not a fundamental solution. Currently, the national weights and measures are being reorganized. The Bureau, in conjunction with the Public Utilities Bureau, has formulated a plan for uniform weights and measures in the city, which has been submitted to the Municipal Government and reported to the Ministry for record. Unification can be expected soon. Furthermore, regarding item (C), concerning the elimination of all improper benefits such as rebates, hu commissions, and transportation subsidies, except for the prescribed commissions for brokers and sales agents, the Bureau has dispatched personnel to investigate rice industry organizations. According to the industry leader Lu Wenshao, the industry originally had no regulations on rebates, hu commissions, or transportation subsidies, which were mostly created secretly by rice merchants from various places at the end of the year when they were eager to settle accounts and return home. If rice merchants can restrain themselves, this type of irregularity can be easily reformed." Based on the aforementioned reasons, the report is submitted for review and referral. In addition to the instructions, this letter is hereby sent for your information.

Three Measures for Managing Traditional Chinese Medicine 116

▲ Proclamation by the Municipal Health Bureau

The Municipal Health Bureau issued a proclamation yesterday to announce the measures for managing traditional Chinese medicine, stating: "For the purpose of proclamation, pursuant to Shanghai Special Municipal Government Instruction No. 4056, approving the Ministry of Health's reply, which was submitted to the National Government for approval, regarding the joint report by the Ministries of Health and Education on the proposed measures for managing traditional Chinese medicine, a copy of the original report is enclosed for your information and compliance. In addition to issuing separate instructions to the Bureau of Education, you are hereby ordered to comply accordingly." Also, an order was received from the Ministry of Health for the same reason. Therefore, a summary of the regulations outlined in the enclosed original report is hereby proclaimed for general knowledge. The proclamation states: (1) Societies aimed at studying traditional Chinese medicine should be called Chinese Medicine Academic Societies, so as to become academic organizations. This measure is to exclude traditional Chinese medicine from the school system, but to allow traditional Chinese medicine to develop freely, without being restricted by educational regulations. In the future, the research of Chinese Medicine Academic Societies will become a precise and systematic theory, and schools will compete to adopt it, without needing to rush to establish schools at present. (2) Traditional Chinese medicine practitioners who do not understand the use of Western instruments and do not know how to sterilize are not allowed to use Western instruments to avoid danger. For example, although traditional Chinese medicine practitioners are allowed to use thermometers, they must be strictly disinfected before being used on others when measuring a patient's temperature, otherwise infectious diseases such as diphtheria and tuberculosis can be transmitted at any time, which is very dangerous. (3) Premises set up by traditional Chinese medicine practitioners to accommodate patients may be called hospitals only if they understand sterilization methods, comply with the regulations for managing hospitals, and have a considerable scale and equipment. The purpose of establishing hospitals is to concentrate patients. If patients are gathered in one hospital and the hospital managers have no knowledge of sterilization, the danger is unspeakable when an acute infectious disease occurs.
