Grandeur of the National Scout General Review 156

Chairman Chiang, Wu Zhihui, and Others' Admonition

121 Scout Troops Attended

▲Afternoon Rest Yesterday Evening Held Campfire

▲Afternoon Performance Today Chiang's Banquet Tomorrow Night

The National Scout General Review was held at Xiaoying, Nanjing on the morning of the 18th at 9:00 AM. Approximately tens of thousands of scouts and visiting guests attended. Chairman Dai Jitao presided over the event. The details of the event are recorded as follows:

A Glimpse of the Venue 157

▲Venue Security

The area around the venue of the conference and the doors near the grandstand are patrolled by the National Government Guard Brigade, police, and scout guards, maintaining order.

▲Grandstand Decoration

The platform is equipped with a radio for speeches and broadcasting orders, and the sound is extremely clear. The entire venue can hear it. The platform has seats for Central Committee members and special guests, marked with red ribbons. Ordinary guests and newspaper reporters are not allowed on the platform. The platform is full of party and national flags, with a portrait of the Premier hung above. Awards presented by important party and state figures and various institutions are displayed in front of the portrait, arranged in three layers, dazzling and eye-catching.

▲Crowded Audience

People from all walks of life in the capital and citizens of the city attended the venue to watch. The venue was crowded with men and women in colorful clothes, leaving almost no space.

▲Venue Couplets

The venue of the conference has couplets hanging, as follows: "The National Boy Scouts should cultivate the new force of the National Revolution under the leadership of our party." "The National Boy Scouts should follow the Premier's teachings and create a new China of the Three Principles of the People." "The National Boy Scouts General Review is to promote future development." "The National Boy Scouts General Review is to examine past achievements." "The Boy Scouts should cultivate the inherent Chinese virtues of wisdom, benevolence, and courage." "The Boy Scouts should abide by the Premier's teachings of love and sincerity."

▲Airplanes Soaring

The Aviation Administration specially dispatched several airplanes to circle the venue of the general review several times before and after the start of the general review, and distributed red and green leaflets. The entire venue of boy scouts cheered thunderously.

▲Attendees

Chiang Kai-shek, Tan Yankai, Dai Jitao, Chiang Menglin, Cai Yuanpei, Gui Chongji, Jiao Yitang, Shao Lizi, Hu Hanmin, Wang Chonghui, Shao Yuanchong, Zhang Zhizhong, Lin Sen, Wu Zhihui, Zhang Mojun, Zhu Peide, Wu Siyu, Miao Bin, Liu Luyin, Zheng Hongnian, Li Shizeng, Gu Yingfen, Ma Fuxiang, Zhang Daofan, Chen Bulei, and many other important figures and their wives attended.

Morning Assembly 158

After 7:00 AM, the chief commander ordered the messengers to issue the first preparation signal. The troop leaders gathered their troops to listen to the orders five minutes before the signal. After hearing the first preparation signal, they led their troops to the review ground and stood at the designated location for their troop. Shortly after, the chief commander ordered the messengers to issue the second preparation signal and sent specialists to inspect each troop. After the specialists reported that everyone was ready, the third preparation signal was issued. The chief commander reported to the chairman, and the chairman approved the start of the meeting and ordered the messengers to issue the first command: "Attention!"

General Review Ceremony 159

1. Joint

2. Entrance

3. First preparation signal

4. Second preparation signal (each troop formed a mouth shape in order)

5. Third preparation signal (each troop lined up to salute)

6. Raising the national flag

7. Singing the party song

8. Paying the highest respect to the party and national flag and the Premier's portrait

9. Chairman respectfully reading the Premier's will

10. Three minutes of silence

11. Reciting the Scout Oath

12. Chairman's report

13. Review

A. Parade

1. Report

2. Inspection

3. Basic exercises

B. Procession

14. Admonition

15. Singing the Scout Song

16. Speech

17. Cheers

A. Long live the Chinese Boy Scouts

B. Long live the Chinese Kuomintang

C. Long live the Republic of China

D. Long live the Three Principles of the People

E. Long live, long live, long live

18. Dismissal

Conference Details 160

At 9:30 AM, the master of ceremonies called for music, and the entire venue was filled with music. After a while, the music stopped, and the master of ceremonies called for everyone to stand at attention. After singing the party song, the flag was raised, and music was played by military bands from the National Government and the municipal government. Then, music was played again. Then, the party and national flags were saluted. Chairman Dai Jitao respectfully read the Premier's will. After reading, there was three minutes of silence. After the silence, the general review began. First, the band played music, and the reporter reported and invited members of the Central Committee to review. Then, he ordered attention, and the military band played music. After the review, they returned to the review stand, and everyone performed basic exercises. Then, the procession began. After the procession was completed, all scouts stood at attention in their predetermined positions to receive admonition. After the admonition, the Scout Song was sung. Then, speeches were given. After the speeches, cheers and slogans were shouted before the troops were dismissed.

Flag Raising Ceremony 161

A flagpole about several feet high was erected in the southeast corner of the venue. After singing the party language at the beginning of the meeting, the flag raising ceremony was held. Staff from the secretariat raised the new flag. The national flag was raised from bottom to top. At this time, the messenger ordered a salute. All scouts holding sticks performed the stick salute, while those empty-handed performed the two-finger salute. The troop flags were tilted 30 degrees to the national flag. Other military police, participants, guests, and spectators also paid tribute to the national flag. The military band played ceremonial music. After the national flag was raised to the top of the flagpole, the messenger ordered the salute to be dismissed.

Parade Details 162

(1) Number of Reported Personnel

The location of each troop in the parade was determined by the office in advance, and signs were erected. The entire troop was arranged in a mouth shape, with each troop divided into rows of small teams. After 7:00 AM, the chief commander ordered the messenger to issue the first preparation signal. Five minutes later, the messenger issued the assembly order. After hearing the assembly order, each troop leader gathered the squad leaders in their respective troops with military signals and ordered them to report the number of personnel being inspected. One minute later, the deputy commander summoned the troop leaders with military signals and ordered them to report the number of personnel being inspected in each troop. One minute later, the chief commander summoned the deputy commanders with military signals and ordered them to report the number of troops under their command and the number of scouts. Then, the chief commander reported to the stage that there were 121 troops in total and 3,366 scouts.

(2) Inspection

After reporting the number of personnel, central representatives and judges set off along the designated inspection route, led by the flag-carrying team. The flag-carrying team was composed of three male and female service personnel, three male and female scouts, three sea scouts, and three cub scouts selected by the chief commander in advance. The leader of the team was the deputy commander, and the flag was in the middle of the first row, carried by service personnel. When starting, the messenger ordered attention. When the inspectors passed each troop, the band played music, and the troop leader ordered a salute. The inspectors returned the salute. The inspectors circled the entire venue along the inspection route and returned to the review stand.

(3) Basic Exercises

After Chairman Chiang and others returned to the review stand, the messenger ordered all scouts to rest. After five minutes, the basic exercises began. At this time, the messenger ordered: 1. Attention, 2. Right dress, 3. Eyes front, 4. Count off, 5. Right face, 6. Left face, 7. At ease. All scouts moved quickly and were full of energy.

Procession Details 163

(1) Messenger Starts

After the exercises were completed, the chief commander reported to the stage that the procession inspection would begin and invited the central representatives to inspect in front of the stage. At the same time, the messenger ordered: 1. Attention, 2. Right face, 3. Forward march. At this time, all scouts began to march.

(2) Circling the Venue Once

When all the scouts began to march, they were led by the deputy commander and the band, and walked past the stage once. When reaching the inspection area, the troop leader ordered "Eyes right." All members looked to the right and passed with goose steps. The troop leaders also performed the salute, and the inspectors returned the salute as required. After all troops passed the inspection area, the troop leaders ordered "Eyes forward," and all members changed to a regular pace and proceeded forward, passing to the left of the command platform and forming a single line according to the predetermined position, standing ready for instruction.

Chairman Chiang's Points of Attention During the Procession and Review 164

▲ Pace, Uniforms, and Next Year's Review, etc.

▲ During the Procession: During the procession, Chairman Chiang and Dai Chuanxian both stood at the entrance of the reviewing stand to conduct the review. Chiang paid close attention to the pace of each scout troop, especially Troops 88, 89, and 111. When these two troops passed the reviewing stand, Chiang inquired about their origins one by one. Staff officers replied with the troop names. Zhang Daofan reported to Chiang that one of the troops was the Nanjing Founding Memorial Boy Scouts, founded by Madam Huang Keqiang and named the "Poor Children's Education and Welfare Home." Subsequently, Chiang and Dai discussed the need to raise more funds for next year's Boy Scout general review to make it better than this year's, advocating for advance preparations. Dai also expressed his opinions. Then, Chiang noticed that the flag of Troop 177 was too low and instructed the staff to raise it higher. He also inquired about the Liangjiang female students in detail.

▲ During the Review: During the review, Chiang, Hu, Dai, Tan, Zhu Peide, Zhang Zhizhong, Wu Siyu, and others went around the field for a full inspection. The scouts saluted when they reached each troop, and Chiang and others returned the salutes accordingly. Chiang paid close attention to the uniforms and postures of each scout and, noting the muddy condition of the field, immediately asked the staff, "Why was it not changed to the airfield for the event?" The staff replied that it was too rushed. Chiang repeatedly said, "Very well, very well." On that day, Chiang wore a military uniform with a large red badge in the center of his left pocket, appearing very energetic. Hu wore a traditional long robe and mandarin jacket, Dai wore a Zhongshan suit, and others wore military uniforms, casual clothes, or Western suits, creating a diverse array of styles.

Chairman Chiang's Address 165

The Three Principles of the People Are the Fundamental Creed of the Boy Scouts

The Goal of Training Is to Create Independent Personalities

Should Abandon Romantic, Frivolous, Decadent, and Treacherous Vices

Do Not Be Blinded by Base, Sordid, and Expedient Mentalities

Performance Results Enrich Spiritual Cultivation

Chairman Chiang delivered an address to the Chinese Boy Scouts yesterday at the venue. His words were as follows: The Chinese Boy Scouts have a history of over ten years since their founding. In the past, they have demonstrated quite good achievements. Since coming under the guidance of our Party, they have a central belief, a unified organization, and practical training, making them even more advanced than before. Judging by the number of participants, there are several thousand participating in this review. Compared with countries like England and the United States, we are indeed far behind, but this also proves that the Chinese Boy Scouts are indeed in the process of development. This first general review of the national Boy Scouts is truly the beginning of a new era for the Chinese Boy Scouts and can be considered an unprecedented grand event in China. I am very happy to participate in this general review and, at the same time, hold infinite hope.

Everyone knows that the Boy Scouts take wisdom, benevolence, and courage as their fundamental spirit. However, this fundamental spirit must have a supreme principle to rely on, and there must be a great mission to which it can be attributed. The Chinese Boy Scouts are named Party Boy Scouts, which indicates that their supreme principle is the Three Principles of the People, and their greatest mission is to realize the Three Principles of the People. The Three Principles of the People are the doctrine of saving the country, the people, and the world. Realizing the Three Principles of the People is realizing the greatest mission of saving the country, the people, and the world. Therefore, the Chinese Boy Scouts must cultivate and develop the spirit of wisdom, benevolence, and courage under the belief of the Three Principles of the People. This is a fundamental creed of our Chinese Boy Scouts. Only those who can abide by this creed are worthy of being Chinese Boy Scouts and worthy of being called Party Boy Scouts.

The humans of the twentieth century should all be members of society and independent individuals. If a person is isolated and acts alone, separating from society, they cannot maintain their survival. If a person relies on others and parasitizes society, they cannot maintain their survival for long. Being able to manage one's own life with one's own strength is being an independent individual. Being able to serve society with one's own strength is being a member of society. Therefore, the goal of Boy Scout training is to create the qualifications of independent individuals and members of society. Training in areas such as first aid, communication, tracking, and etiquette is training in serving society. Skills such as washing, sewing, and cooking are techniques for managing one's own life with one's own strength. If these training sessions are skilled and last for a long time, they will naturally become a kind of social person with an independent spirit. Among them, the most important thing is the spirit of united living. If every member of a Boy Scout leaves his group, he loses his function, and at the same time, his group also loses a share of strength. Therefore, the group life of the Boy Scouts is organic and extremely close. If human society can reach this level, it will definitely be very developed and advanced. The training of the Boy Scouts is to expand this spirit of strictly divided group life to social life, so that society becomes an organic and close society. The Premier of our Party once said that people are endowed with a natural nature of being in groups, but it must be trained before the nature of being in groups can progress. This is one of the most important goals of Boy Scout training.

The purpose of the Chinese revolution is to build a society based on the Three Principles of the People. A society based on the Three Principles of the People is an organized, disciplined, and strict society, not a free and loose society. However, the Chinese people's looseness and dilapidation have reached their extreme. If it is not subjected to strict training, this organized and disciplined society based on the Three Principles of the People can never be realized. The people of the past era are already difficult to correct. Youth are the masters of the country in the future and the backbone of society. Therefore, the only hope for China lies in youth. However, because of the poor social environment, most of the youth in China are now romantic, frivolous, decadent, and treacherous, only knowing personal freedom and not abiding by group discipline, indulging in pleasure and disregarding everything. If this phenomenon is allowed to continue, China's future will only lead to national subjugation and racial extinction. Therefore, in this transitional era of revolution, the Boy Scouts are an urgently needed organization. Those who join the Boy Scouts now are all young people over the age of twelve, not far from adulthood. If they can receive sufficient and strict training during this period, they will definitely become the backbone of the new society after they reach adulthood. Therefore, the responsibility of building a society based on the Three Principles of the People rests on the shoulders of every member of our Boy Scouts. Therefore, every member of the Boy Scouts should strive to eliminate all bad habits such as romanticism, frivolity, decadence, and treachery, cultivate the spirit of respecting the group and obeying discipline, abide by the Premier's last words, "Only the group has freedom, individuals have no freedom," and create a model of Chinese youth.

In the revolutionary process, the mission of the Party Boy Scouts is particularly important compared to the Boy Scouts of other countries. Its nature can be said to be a reserve army for the revolutionary ranks. Its mission is to complete the great cause of the National Revolution. Every member is a young revolutionary fighter. His thoughts must be pure and not shaken by heresies other than the Three Principles of the People. His motives must be pure, and he must not be blinded by any base, sordid, or expedient mentalities. He must have a spirit of self-improvement and self-reliance, and the perseverance to endure hardship and hard work. He should not pursue superficial vanity but should seek inner enrichment. Only in this way can he be worthy of being called a revolutionary youth, and only in this way can he shoulder difficult and enormous responsibilities. It is necessary for every member to be trained to this level, and then the mission of the Boy Scouts can be considered to have been completed.

Now, because of financial and other difficulties, the Chinese Boy Scouts are limited to a part of the students in schools. However, in the future, we must find ways to expand and develop them. Not only students in schools but also the youth of the general public in society should have the opportunity to join them. Then the training can be universal, and the effect can be great. This is my hope for those in charge of running the Boy Scouts.

I am more pleased to participate in this general review today than to review the army because I see these thousands of innocent and lively young people as if there are thousands of strands of hope placed before me, so I am very moved and very gratified. I hope that if any shortcomings are found as a result of this review, we should try our best to improve them. If, by the time of the second review, the members' belief in the doctrine can be deepened, the achievements of service performance can be further improved, and the cultivation of the spirit can be further enriched, then the future of China will have infinite hope. Finally, I wish the Chinese Boy Scouts a long life.

Wu Zhihui's Address 166

▲ Boy Scouts should struggle equally

▲ Protect yourselves, protect your nation

Brothers, today I see the National Boy Scouts gathering together. I recall that when I first went to England, I did not know English. At that time, I met Premier Sun Yat-sen and saw a Boy Scout. The Premier said, "This is a Boy Scout." Later, when I went to Scotland, I said, "These are the people of Scotland." The Zhongshan suit invented by the Premier is the uniform of the Boy Scouts. The purpose is to transform the elderly into Boy Scouts, wearing arms, which is a convenience for a collective group, for peace, struggle, and saving China. This is the revolutionary purpose of the Premier. The Chinese Boy Scouts should use peace and struggle to implement Chinese nationalism. The Boy Scouts should manage everything themselves. Anything in the world can be Boy Scoutized to protect themselves and their nation, and promote world harmony. This is your responsibility. You should gather the Chinese people together, use persuasion and struggle methods, and achieve the goal of saving China peacefully as the Premier said, and eliminate all reactionary warlords in the country. This is my little wish for the Chinese Boy Scouts, a hundred million years.

Cai Yuanpei's Address 167

▲ Emphasize struggle, sacrifice, independence, and mutual assistance

In short, today, taking the opportunity of the National Boy Scout General Review, I would like to offer a few suggestions to all comrades. According to the regulations of the Boy Scouts, the main points are nothing more than "struggle, sacrifice, independence, and mutual assistance." Boy Scouts must have the strength to struggle in order to be independent, and they must have the spirit of sacrifice in order to help each other. The Three Principles of the People written by the Premier are also aimed at making each of us have the strength to struggle and the spirit of sacrifice to practice the virtues of independence and mutual assistance. What each comrade must understand today is that the total number of National Boy Scouts is over 13,000, but only over 3,000 can come today. What is the reason? We must know that those who cannot come to Beijing are actually subject to various obstacles and preventions. We should practice mutual assistance, use the strength of struggle and the spirit of sacrifice to break these obstacles, so that when the second general review is held, all the National Boy Scouts can come to Beijing to participate. We must also help the majority of other young people to receive this kind of training so that all the people in the country have the spirit of "struggle, sacrifice, independence, and mutual assistance."

Dai Chuanxian's Address 168

▲ Training Boy Scouts is a good medicine for saving the Chinese nation

Comrades, the first National Boy Scout General Review and Jamboree convened by the Central Government is the first day today. Just now, during the review, seeing such a large-scale assembly of the first general review and such a unified spirit, I feel very satisfied. However, I still hope that all of you, no matter which group you are in, must remember for yourselves that you must know where you should seek improvement and where you should seek progress in the future. You must continue to work hard to train until the second review next year, and you will have better results. At the same time, in terms of substance and quantity, there will be greater expansion. Today, taking this opportunity, I would like to state my personal opinions to you. We deeply know that the Chinese nation is extremely weak. For more than a thousand years, it has been oppressed by those barbaric and tyrannical nations. In the eras of the Six Dynasties, the Five Dynasties, and the Mongol and Manchu Dynasties, the oppression was even more severe. Why is such a large nation-state so unlucky? In the recent hundred years or so, it has suffered even more severely from the oppression of imperialists. Under this kind of situation, how should we work hard to become strong? To put it simply to you, when China was strong and prosperous, it was called a first-class country and nation. Wherever people and vehicles could reach in the whole world, no matter who they were, they all respected the Chinese people. It can be said that they paid tribute every year and came to court every year. The reason for this is that China is a country of etiquette and a civilized country. The so-called etiquette is like all the etiquette and organizations and human feelings established by the country, which can be said to be etiquette. The so-called righteousness is that everything, no matter how big or small, is handled well, which is called righteousness. Being able to sacrifice to help others can also be called the virtue of righteousness. The reason why our country is called a country of etiquette and righteousness is that our people can stand out from all nations without using military oppression, but taking the protection of civilization. But today, what is our status? The total number of National Boy Scouts is only over 13,000. Taking China's population of 400 million as a proportion, that is, only one in 40,000 can receive this kind of education, that is, only one in tens of thousands of people is a Boy Scout. Comrades, think about how many Chinese people can read and write? How many more people can go to higher or vocational schools? This kind of proportion is really chilling. At the same time, I ask all comrades to pay attention to the actions of a group of people after they return to their hometowns. Most of them are disrespectful when they meet, and they even curse other people's parents and ancestors. The people of the so-called country of etiquette and righteousness should help up those who stumble and rescue those who fall into the water. But now, most people not only do not help up those who stumble or rescue those who fall into the water, but they also clap and laugh on the sidelines. This kind of habit is exposing that China's original etiquette and righteousness have been lost. Now, we hope that all Boy Scouts will pay attention to this kind of bad habit and correct it after they return to their hometowns. We must make people everywhere have a spirit of mutual assistance, and all actions must be polite, creating a civilized country with etiquette and righteousness. This kind of education and training for Boy Scouts is really a good medicine for the Chinese nation to be reborn. Comrades, seeing such an important duty, you should strive forward to save China. After the address, the slogan was cheered several times, and the meeting was dismissed at 12:30.

Cheers at the Venue 169

After the speeches, the entire venue cheered: 1. Long live the Chinese Boy Scouts! 2. Long live the Chinese Kuomintang! 3. Long live the Republic of China! 4. Long live the Three Principles of the People! 5. Long live! Long live! Long live! The sound shook the entire venue.

Announcement of the End of the Meeting 170

After the speeches, the commander-in-chief announced the end of the meeting and ordered each group leader to lead his group of Boy Scouts to the campsite for rest.

Afternoon Situation Yesterday 171

Because the Boy Scouts were tired from the general review in the morning, they rested for half a day in the afternoon. The group leaders organized the internal affairs of their groups. A bonfire was held in the evening.

Bonfire Party Last Night 172

On the evening of the 18th, the second morning of the National Boy Scout Jamboree, after the general review, the guests had already gathered. After the meeting reported that they would rest in the afternoon and organize the campsite, the guests gradually withdrew. At 6:00 PM, the campsite was extremely crowded with guests. The bonfire party is a unique performance method for Boy Scouts during camping. Although Boy Scouts from various places have held it during camping, this is the first time that a Chinese Boy Scout bonfire party has been held. The grand occasion at that time is recorded in detail as follows: The meeting started at 8:00 PM. The guests and all the Boy Scouts formed a large circle. For a while, the flames were blazing, and the smoke was rising into the sky. The group performances began. The first was the English singing of Troop 196. The song was "Over There," with melodious twists and turns, which can be called wonderful. The second was the mouth and nose music of Troop 92 from Xiamen Jimei, with amazing rhythm. The third was the comical dance of Troop 61, with strange costumes, which was praised by the entire venue. The fourth was the singing of Troop 119 from Nanyang Middle School. First, each person held a fire and ran into the venue, circling it once. Then, they cheered "Long live China" and played three "Homesick" songs on the harmonica. The entire venue applauded thunderously. The fifth was the five-minute "Touch Touch" of Troop 78. One person placed several paper notes in a bag. Each person had to touch one and perform according to the name of the game written on the paper note, such as telling a story, performing a set of boxing, or singing a section of "The Empty City Stratagem." The sixth was the dance of Troop 121 from Shanghai Southeast Women's Physical Education College. The dance was called the "Bullfight Dance," which made everyone laugh. The seventh was the joke of Troop 117. The eighth was the boxing of Troop 197, namely Gao Junqiu from Liangjiang Women's Physical Education College performing a set of "Five-Road Chaquan." The ninth was the boxing of Troop 113, with Wu Xueying performing a set of sword dance. There were many other performances.

Order for Today and Tomorrow 173

The General Review Office held the third and fourth administrative meetings on the afternoon of the 18th. The issue of the Boy Scout performance time was discussed. It was decided that the Boy Scouts would hold lectures, fellowship meetings, and visits on their own in the mornings of the 19th and 20th. Performances would be held from 1:00 PM to 4:30 PM in the afternoon. Bonfires would be held from 7:00 PM to 9:00 PM in the evening. A visit to the mausoleum would be held on the morning of the 20th.

Banquet Tomorrow Night 174

▲ Chairman Chiang will host a banquet in the name of the Lixingshe

Chiang sent a letter to the office in the name of the president of the Lixingshe, setting the banquet for Boy Scout officers and squad leaders at the Lixingshe at 6:00 PM on the evening of the 20th.

Sports

News of Our Country's Preparations for the Far Eastern Games 175

▲ Athletes will travel to Suzhou this morning: About one hundred male and female athletes, led by Hao Boyang, the main person in charge of the Sports Promotion Association, and coaches, will travel to Suzhou by car at 7:00 this morning. They will return to Shanghai at 5:00 or 6:00 that evening. ▲ Continued donations to the Games fund: The funds required to attend the Far Eastern Games this time are very large. In addition to the 20,000 yuan funded by the National Government, the rest is raised from all parties. The results are still good. Yesterday, it was learned that Lin Zhuguang, a warm-hearted overseas Chinese in the Philippines who is enthusiastic about sports, personally donated 1,000 yuan and promised to raise funds there on his behalf. Tan Yasheng also donated 500 yuan.

▲ Additional recruitment of volunteer coaches: The former competition board decided that if there are Westerners in Shanghai with rich sports experience, they can be asked to help. Our country has telegraphed to invite Ms. Mudan and Ms. Xinghua to return to China to attend the Far East and win glory for the country.

▲ Scheduled practice trials

Experts are being hired for each sport to start training. The Preparatory Office plans to hold a trial competition on May 6 to examine the track and field results. Field event referee Yu Jie, track event referee Shi Xiangzai, starter Liu Chongsi, inspector Xu Minhui, timers Guo Yubin, Zhao Zhanyuan, Xia Xianze, Wu Zhi, Fang Songjunfu, Xu Shaowu, recorder Wang Shoufang, Ji Yuan, etc.

Jiangnan University Sports Association to Hold Sports Meet 177

▲Next Month, 3rd and 4th

▲At the Chinese Athletic Field

The track and field competition committee of the Jiangnan University Sports Association has decided to hold a sports meet on May 3rd and 4th at the Chinese Athletic Field on Route Pères Froc (present-day Tianlin Road). The resolutions of the committee are recorded below:

(1) The Jiangnan University Track and Field Sports Meet is scheduled to take place on May 3rd and 4th from 1:00 PM onwards at the Chinese Athletic Field on Route Pères Froc.

(2) Registration is open from now until 6:00 PM on April 30th. Register with Wang Fudan at Guanghua University in Shanghai.

(3) The association will award a shield to the winner of the championship.

(4) The rules of each event will follow the standards of the 8th Far Eastern Games. (5) Central University will be responsible for arranging their own accommodation and meals in Shanghai.

(6) The official track and field competition events and their order are as follows:

(1) 100 meters (2) Shot put (3) 800 meters (4) High jump (5) 200 meters (6) Discus throw (7) 110-meter hurdles (8) 3000 meters (9) Long jump (10) 400 meters (11) Javelin throw (12) 200-meter low hurdles (13) Triple jump (14) 1500 meters (15) Pole vault (16) 800-meter relay (17) 1600-meter medley relay (18) Pentathlon (19) Decathlon

(7) For each event, except the relays and pentathlon/decathlon, points are awarded as follows: 5 points for 1st place, 4 points for 2nd place, 3 points for 3rd place, 2 points for 4th place, and 1 point for 5th place. For the pentathlon and decathlon, points are awarded as follows: 10 points for 1st place, 8 points for 2nd place, 6 points for 3rd place, 4 points for 4th place, and 2 points for 5th place. Relays do not count towards the score. However, if two or more schools have the same total score, the championship and ranking will be determined by the order of finish in the relays.

(8) Each athlete can participate in a maximum of four events. Athletes participating in the pentathlon or decathlon, or both, cannot participate in other events.

(9) Each school can enter a maximum of five athletes per event.

(10) The committee will appoint the referees.

A Laughing Matter 182

— Hai Ke

▲A: Why don't you send your son to school to study?

B: You know I own a southern goods store. We often use twelve taels as a pound. But the math teacher at that school teaches him to use sixteen taels as a pound. Isn't that clearly trying to harm us?

▲Woman: Your talk of love is completely fake. Your heart is fake. Even your smile is fake. Everything about you is fake.

Man: Yes, as fake as your set of false teeth.

▲Woman: Do you remember when you first proposed to me, I rejected you?

Man: Thank you. That's my sweetest memory.

▲Shopkeeper (reproaching a clerk): Hey! You should be more polite when serving customers in the future. That lady just came to tell me that you didn't give her a pleasant look.

Clerk: But I brought out all the goods in the shop for her to see!

▲A: He has such an ugly face, yet he thinks he's a handsome young man.

B: We should punish him.

A: What kind of punishment?

B: Print his photo in all the major newspapers, with the caption "World's Most Handsome Young Man, [Name]."

Anecdotes of American Minister Johnson 183

— Qiu Shui

According to foreign news reports, the anecdotes of American Minister Johnson are quite detailed. The original author has lived in Beiping for a long time and is a close friend of Johnson's, so what he says should not be false. Here is my translation of it:

▲Rickshaw Obsession: Johnson likes to ride rickshaws in China, especially in Beiping, and doesn't like to ride motorcars. Except for occasional urgent official business, he will drive a car. When he goes to banquets or leisure activities, a rickshaw is indispensable. Johnson once said to someone: "Watching the scenery from a car is like glancing at flowers from horseback, with no enjoyment at all. It's better to hire a rickshaw and walk slowly, which is more suitable." Also, Johnson is very polite to the rickshaw pullers he hires. He always pays more than others. Along the way, he likes to chat with the rickshaw pullers, not considering himself an official. Rickshaw pullers in the Dongjiaominxiang area of ​​Beiping all know Johnson, but very few of them know that he is the American minister to China.

▲Fondness for Black Bow Ties: At various banquets in Beiping, if the head of the embassy is present, guests must wear evening dress. However, Johnson is not used to this. He often wears a regular suit with a black bow tie. He also often talks about this with people in the embassy, ​​strenuously advocating the black bow tie doctrine. If there is a banquet one evening that requires him to wear full dress, Johnson often asks a friend halfway through to remove the full dress and replace it with the same clothing so that when all the guests gather, they will not find Johnson strange.

▲Hatamen Cigarette Obsession: Johnson has another special hobby, that is, he usually doesn't smoke cigarettes, but if he smokes cigarettes, he must smoke Hatamen cigarettes. Hatamen is a medium-grade tobacco, very cheap, and is smoked by ordinary coolies. It is strange that Johnson is addicted to it. Johnson once told Chinese friends when he came to China again: "China is my second motherland. I feel very happy to come to China this time. One of the reasons for my happiness is that I can taste Hatamen again. Because Hatamen cigarettes are only sold in China, and there is no way to buy them in the United States." Some people explain Johnson's Hatamen obsession by saying that Johnson used to smoke Hatamen cigarettes when he was a student translator in China, so he became addicted. Later, he felt that the taste was still the same as before, so he couldn't help but become addicted.

A Visit to Ye Garden 184

— Zhu Ming

It is better to visit the garden when it is sunny. However, the garden after the rain has more flavor to savor. On April 12th, I participated in a visit to Ye Garden initiated by the Youth Association. On this day, the sky was dim, and the chaotic clouds seemed to be raining, but the enthusiasm of the visitors did not diminish. After lunch, we went by car. When we arrived in Jiangwan, the raindrops were already like threads. When we arrived at the garden, the rain was like a tide. The guests all looked for pavilions to shelter from the rain. Between the flying beads and jade, one stone, one flower, one bridge, and one willow were all full of picturesque interest. Its intriguing part is not in the sunny buildings, pavilions, and lakeside pavilions. More than half past two o'clock, tourists gathered on the lawn in the eastern corner of the garden. The person in charge of the Youth Association gave a speech, followed by the national music of the Yousheng Traveling Troupe. I specially led away to the water near the wall to listen to it. The wind passed, and the sound came, not like listening to the sound of the flute in the bamboo under the moon. The music stopped for a gentleman to dance the sword, and the photography was at the end. For a while, the skirts flew, laughing and talking, making people forget the sound of war drums in the Central Plains. Ye Yuan's victory is that in the shade of the bridge and by the water, there are several weeping willows, and several stones lying down between the willows and the waves. If the tourists lift up their clothes and wade in the stream, and stand in the depths of the green waves, they should feel cool and green in the shadow of the small bridge and the chaotic willows in the lake. When I visited Liuyuan in Wuzhong last autumn, I saw artists in Wuzhong painting old trees, horizontal branches, low walls, and chaotic rocks at Yuantouzhu. I also saw people painting flat waves, distant trees, green ridges, and windy sails. However, the customs here are not as good as those of Liangxi in Wuxia. It should be given to the old painter in the spring river, and the green teenagers should not be allowed to open their cameras in their arms and laugh at people. On the way back, I felt inspired and composed a small verse in Lian Yuan to record this Qing tour. Arriving at the door, the rain washes away the fragrance and dust, and the weeping willows condense their green waists. The sound of birds cries, flying catkins fill the courtyard, and a bay of flowing water. Junlu is unrestrained, leaving shadows while walking in the green, and leaning on the painted railing together. Laughter is hurriedly spent picking vegetables, who should be asked to connect with the spring marks? The tender agreement is still remembered. It is so soul-destroying that the curtains are empty and green, crying red and weeping dew, the flowers are dim and the willows are dim, and the two flavors. Try dancing with Wu Gou, wait for Yue Niang to be poured, and Mu Jia will rise again. Another Xiao sings out new sorrows like the sea, and puts the East Wind against him.

A Record of Mr. Li Yie, a Native of Heshan 185

— Li Shiyuan

In recent years, thanks to the efforts of General Li Jinglin and Committee Members Chu Minyi in promoting martial arts, people everywhere have followed suit and are competing to practice national martial arts as a pleasure. However, Mr. Li Yie, a national martial artist who was highly praised by General Li ten years ago, was also a sharpshooter (Mr. Li was famous for his marksmanship) who once served as the magistrate of Heshan County. Mr. Li was skilled in fighting, somersaulting, and leaping. His movements were as fast as an eagle or falcon. He often wore simple clothing and short jackets. He would adopt a horse-riding posture with his knees forward, and several people could stand on his legs without him showing any sign of strain. He is old, but his spirit is vigorous, just like when he was young. When he governed Heshan County, which was plagued by bandits, for more than a year, the thieves warned each other not to enter. One day, a relative of his was celebrating his son's wedding and sent a letter inviting him to attend the banquet. More than a hundred thieves gathered and rushed forward with shouts. Just as the gatekeeper reported that Mr. Li had arrived, the thieves were all speechless and said, "We've ruined our plan. We can't offend the sharpshooter!" In an instant, they scattered like birds and beasts. Such was Mr. Li's power and people's respect for him.

Five years ago, when Mr. Li heard the news of the death of Sun Yat-sen, the great revolutionary, he wept bitterly. He wrote a eulogy in his own hand: "The Central Plains are troubled, and I grieve in vain" "The mountain and the Big Dipper gaze vainly at the withered sage." The words "Zhongshan" (Sun Yat-sen's name) were incorporated into the couplet, almost seamlessly. I have included it here as a special note.

Chrysanthemum Talk in Tianjin 186

— Xu Xiaoting, from Tianjin

I have been in Tianjin for a week, and I have been traveling with my old friend Sha Youtian to sing in the theater. Now I will write down the latest news I have received about the chrysanthemum world.

Yanqiu has shaved his beard and stopped singing in Shanghai. Tianjin also says the same thing, and some say that Cheng (Yanqiu) had no choice but to do so to avoid the limelight of the new Yanqiu. It is inevitable that Yu Shuang will be tarnished. Cheng once came to Tianjin with his chrysanthemum friends Shou Chen and Miaoxiang to perform last month. This statement is self-defeating. Youtian told Yu, "Yanqiu has indeed become ill and fat. The color pants have been let out three times at the waist. His voice is gradually loosening. The wide sounds often contain harsh sounds. He can no longer control his voice as freely as he used to. His appearance has not been damaged. This time, Cheng is very willing to work hard for the sake of his own reputation. As a result, the results are still good." After Cheng returned to Ping, he formed his own team and invited Furongcao to join. The momentum is very strong. Now the Tianjin Butterfly Grand Theater has scheduled Cheng Ling to perform Biyu Zan and Jin Suoji on the evenings of April 19th and 20th. Advertisements have been posted for many days. The words "Cheng Opera" are specially marked to appeal to the public. It can be seen that people are enthusiastically welcoming Yanqiu.

Wang Shaolou is a promising successor to Sheng. His voice is excellent. His singing is very similar to Shuyan. He is very skilled in his body. He acts very seriously. The only thing that is lacking is his recitation. He once performed in Tianjin for a month. He was a big hit. Later, he sang with Xue Yanqin at Chunhe for four days. Tickets were sold out in advance. Tomorrow (the 11th), he will perform with Xue Ling, Shou Chen, and Ruian at Chunhe for three days. The ticket price is as high as two yuan. The plays are Wang Hao's Shen Pan Hong Xue Zhou's Farewell Ji. (first night) Wang Xue's Kill Home. Xue Zhou Hao's Ci Shen. (second night) Zhou Hao's Chang Ban Po. Wang Xue Hao's Famen Temple. (third day) Zhou Hao's Steal the Imperial Horse. Wang Xue's Run Slope Deng Dian. (third night) The grand occasion can be predicted. Huang Quansheng of Shanghai Grand Theater originally wanted to invite Yanqiu to go south, but Cheng allowed him to perform in the second half of the year. Huang then intended to change the contract with Wang Xue or Wang Yu (Cuihua). According to Shaolou, Yu Nanhang is still waiting for the final consideration. He must be sure that he is sure to succeed before he can act. However, in terms of Shaolou's art, this trip will not be unfavorable. If he can bring Tongchui Shuoguo Qiu Guixian together, two unfamiliar faces, they will definitely be seated. Only Danjue needs to be considered.

Fu Ying is singing a farewell commemorative play at the Zhongyuan Company. The attendance is good. Xiaopei is also invited to accompany him in the play "Ganlu Temple" as Qiao Guolao and Lu Su. The Danjue is Hu Bilan, who is praised by the Peilan Society. This Zhi has recently become a disciple of Xiaoyun and sings more solidly and correctly. Among the Kunjue, she is the most pleasant to listen to. However, her smoky face does not seem appropriate. After Fuying's term expires, Zhongyuan has scheduled the martial arts master Yang Xiaolou to sing solo for several days. Then he hired Huisheng or Xiaoyun to take over the team. There will definitely be a lively time at that time.

An Shuyuan has changed from Xinming Theater to Xinxin Stage. This gentleman is well-connected in Tianjin. However, his voice is deteriorating day by day, and many people regret it. In addition, there are the old brand Bangzi of Tianfeng Garden and the Kunban of Kuideshe Theater in Xinxin Theater, which are lined up to rely on marriage and new family dramas. They are all slightly seated. Tian Hua Jing is the territory of the Kunling Qiluan Jiao and Huang Runqing's son, Tongling Binsheng Huang Chu Bao. (Recompense)

Warmth in My Heart (174) 187

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 10: Red Flames Soar to the Sky: the Filial Daughter of Goulan; Red Carpet on the Ground: the Renowned Actress Impromptu

A Jin said: "I didn't expect Miss Wen Guizhi to be so conscientious." "They say she was born as a prostitute." A Bao said: "She is the best prostitute. Those second-rate prostitutes can't compare to her." A Jin said: "I suppose that old woman must be her grandmother." "If she were adopted, how could she be so filial?" A Bao said: "I heard them say that Miss Wen Guizhi's mother died when she was young. She died a month after giving birth to her. Her mother got a postpartum disease. Her grandmother raised her. She never ate well because she was sick since she was born. She was fed a little milk powder. She was raised like this. Her father specializes in drinking and gambling. He sold her in the Jie Er Tang. Fortunately, she was born beautiful. She was also lucky. She jumped to Chang San. So she never forgets her grandmother. This is called being born and raised by herself. She is conscientious after all." They said these two sentences, looking at this Aunt Da and looking at Ruiyun and other purchased servants, and felt that these words were a bit taboo. So they stopped talking. The topic turned to another place, saying: "This time, Miss Wen Gui has suffered a lot of losses. Not to mention the jewelry, they don't have a small house. All the things have to be placed in the business. Even the clothes in the hall will feel unfashionable in a year or two. But when you make them, they are expensive. It is not easy to make all the single-layered cotton and leather clothes now. I don't know if they have insured them. If they have insured them, it would be better after all. Even if the compensation is not enough, half of it will be taken." Aunt Da said: "Who would insure the hall?" "Because we often have to move. We often live for two or three sections and then move to another place. Isn't it troublesome to insure? If you have a small house, it is worth insuring. This year, a customer agreed to me to insure. Looking at this, I have the idea of insuring. It only costs a dozen taels of silver a year. You can insure three thousand taels of silver. It is reassuring." A Bao said: "I heard that Miss Wen Guizhi has a good customer. They say his surname is Yan. Everyone calls him Lord Yan. He is a Daotai. But when he walks, one foot is a bit limping. People also There is a call to him Yan Jiaojiao. It is said that he ate a bullet when he was fighting the East." "This Lord Yan is very rich. Now that the things have been burned, is he afraid that Lord Yan will not compensate her? Today, he just came back from Lord Yan's Tang. With such a good customer, it is better than insurance."

Random Notes on Touring America at Zhuiyu Studio 188

— Lai

Since the move last week, the seats have remained full. It has now been decided to change the repertoire in the fourth week (i.e., the second week after the move). It was originally planned to change to Naoxue, Luhua Dang, Yu Wu, and Dayu Shajia. Now, because the Japanese opera opened last night, the New York newspapers all say that it is not as calm as the Chinese opera. Moreover, the audience here applauds the most for the sword dance and Guifang's exit with a knife. However, the commentators in the newspaper praised Fenhewan Ci Hu. Since our opera has won praise for its calmness, we will certainly work hard on calmness in the future. Therefore, it is planned to change the repertoire. The final decision is as follows: First, the Drunkenness section. Second, Luhua Dang. Third, Xishi's feather dance. Fourth, Dayu Shajia. The above four operas have been carefully considered and rehearsed several times. We will wait for the dress rehearsal on Sunday night and ask people from all walks of life to visit, watch, and criticize.

The opera community recently invited Wan and others to a dinner. More than 500 people attended. Wan gave a speech. The association also presented Wan and all the members of the troupe with honorary membership certificates. This is also a first for the New York Drama Association.

Recently, all the famous actors, both old and young, have come to watch the opera. They all came to the backstage to meet and express their respect. One famous actor said: "A woman's drunkenness is very difficult to watch. Chinese opera can describe it to such an extent. It is really unimaginable." From this, we can know the depth of the Chinese opera organization and the exquisiteness of Mei Jun's art. Several old ladies watched Dayu Shajia and said, "Chinese girls are really good. No matter how unwilling they are, they have to compromise and please their fathers. American girls will never accommodate people." This is probably a feeling.

Yesterday, I met with Mr. Yang again. We had a very pleasant conversation. Mr. Yang said: "The organization of Mr. Mei's visit to the United States is the most appropriate. The publicity is also just right. In the past, some foreigners came here and failed because the publicity was excessive and the name did not match the reality. There are quite a few people. This time, all the measures are very appropriate. I will write a letter to China to praise it." Then he asked which newspaper would be appropriate. When he told them that the major newspapers in Shanghai, Tianjin, and Ping could, he said that he would disclose the information in a letter soon. He also said that the appearance of Dayu Shajia was extremely beautiful. It was completely Chinese style. Wan Hua is always friendly, so he also said: "One person has achieved such a great reputation, and is still so humble. How can he not become a world figure? I admire this very much. And American famous actors are often complacent and arrogant. But this time they are not proud of Mr. Mei at all."

Financial Closing Slightly Weak 189

Yesterday was a bank holiday, so the financial market was relatively quiet. The market price of silver ingots was 72.15 cents in the morning and 72.1625 cents in the afternoon. The interest rate for silver was 2 cents in both the morning and afternoon. The amount of foreign exchange drawn was 585,000 in the morning and 795,000 in the afternoon. Banknotes were 5,000 in the morning and 15,000 in the afternoon. Outside the exchange, banknotes were 44,000 in the morning and 30,000 in the afternoon. Silver dollars were 118,000 in the morning and 65,000 in the afternoon. Banks collected over 2.4 million in foreign exchange and over 23 million in silver. Small money shops traded 400,000 to 500,000 in banknotes, drafts, and silver dollars. Silver Prices Rise in London, Steady in America 191

Yesterday, April 18th (Friday), was the Western Qingming Festival, and customs and foreign banks were closed for four days. Therefore, there were no reports on the gold or foreign exchange markets. However, according to London telegrams, the price of silver had rebounded, with the near-term increasing by 0.0625 and the long-term increasing by 0.125, both to 19 pence 6875. There was a small amount of buying by India, and the market was flat. According to a New York telegram, the price of American silver remained unchanged, at 42.625 cents. The British pound fell by 0.15625 against the US dollar, to $4.861875. The US dollar fell by 0.09375 against the British pound, to $4.863125. The Japanese yen remained at 49.375. The British pound remained at 2 shillings 0.40621. The British shilling in Shanghai remained at 1 shilling 11 pence 4375. The Bombay spot price increased by 2 angres, to 55 rupees 02. Later, a telegram at 10:25 AM reported that it had risen by another 4 angres, to 55 rupees 06 angres.

Bond Market Slightly Calmer 193

▲Reorganization of the Sixth Year Loan Rises Again, Turnover Exceeds 5.9 Million

Yesterday, the Shanghai bond market saw a total turnover of 19,700 yuan in spot trading. Excluding the reorganization loan, which accounted for 13,700 yuan, other bonds only amounted to a few thousand yuan. The futures market was far from its previous activity. Market sentiment was calm, with total daily turnover not exceeding 6 million yuan. Among these, Customs Bonds accounted for the largest share, totaling 2.2 million yuan. The Reorganization of the Sixth Year Loan also saw 1.4 million yuan in turnover. Other significant volumes included 700,000 yuan for Internal Rehabilitation Bonds, 400,000 yuan each for Continued Consolidation Loan and Reorganization Loan, 265,000 yuan for Disbandment Bonds, 155,000 yuan for the 1996 Bonds, and only 55,000 yuan for the Seventh Year Loan. The Financial Bond market saw no activity throughout the day.

The price trends of various bonds were generally stable, fluctuating within a narrow range without significant changes. The Continued Consolidation Loan, Seventh Year Loan, and 1996 Bonds only fluctuated by a few cents, with minimal changes compared to the previous day. However, the Reorganization of the Sixth Year Loan and Disbandment Bonds saw their prices rebound due to active buying interest in the market, rising by about one yuan compared to the previous day. Furthermore, the spot price of the Disbandment Bonds suddenly opened higher, rising by 4.8 yuan compared to last week.

Yarn and Cotton Market News 194

Yarn and Flower: The Yarn Market Remains in Chaos 195

The yarn market fell in the morning but rebounded in the afternoon, with an extremely scattered trend. This is due to the unfavorable environment, many rumors in the current situation, and weak investor sentiment. Sales of current yarn are becoming increasingly bleak, primarily due to the impending deadline, leading to a generally bearish outlook. However, major buyers are holding firm and unwilling to loosen their grip, even showing interest in taking delivery. Simultaneously, short sellers are aggressively seeking out current yarn in the market, creating intense competition between the bulls and bears. Based on the overall trend, the price of 512 at 32 taels temporarily appears to have the possibility of stabilizing.

▲ Futures Yarn Falls and Rises Again: Pre-market opening saw the shorts cover 1,000 bales of ten-count yarn from the previous day, causing investor sentiment to loosen and selling pressure to increase, with prices for each month falling by 0.1, 0.2, 0.4, 0.5, and 0.7 mace. In the afternoon, buyers saw that the current month's pre-market closing had reached the limit price of 52 taels, so they purchased another 200 bales, slightly shaking market sentiment. Retail investors covered their short positions, causing prices to rebound by 0.1, 0.2, and 0.3 mace. However, trading was sparse, with a total daily turnover of only 6,400 lots.

Grain: River Rice Market Languishes 198

▲ Zhabei: Yesterday, there were very few ships arriving from various guilds, and sales suddenly turned sluggish. Changbang white japonica rice was weak due to poor buying interest, down a few cents. Zhongguan secondary japonica rice was also slow. Recently, ordinary japonica rice prices have changed very quickly, with market transactions fluctuating by one or two cents. The overall market situation felt weak and tired. Thin rice and early rice were originally firm, but now there are few customers. Although river stocks are not large, the atmosphere is weakening, and prices have been slightly reduced. Yangdu pointed rice sales were flat in the morning, and goods were also scarce. The overall market was soft in the midst of stability. At noon, it was heard that foreign rice was doing well again. In general, local indica rice is not easy to sell. Metamorphosed Yuan Yin rice is also dull. Sales are limited, and the market is short by nearly a cent.

▲ Huinan: There are also few sources from the river, but market sales are not smooth. High-quality machine-milled japonica rice sales are quiet, and transactions are very small. Su Tong machine-milled japonica rice sales are still acceptable, but buyers are eager to cut prices, while sellers are unwilling to reduce prices. Initially, there was an appearance of mutual rejection. Then, due to the soft report from the Zhabei market, there was a slight reduction in wholesale prices. However, in fact, japonica rice prices here are difficult to fall back. Thin rice and southern early rice sources are scarce, sales are normal, and market conditions are slightly flat in the afternoon. Currently, after the establishment of the Peace Preservation Committee, buyers are mostly watching and waiting. Yangdu pointed rice arrivals are few, and the market is very stable. Coupled with the support of foreign rice, the situation is still good. Buying interest in hundred-yuan rice is deserted, with only sporadic transactions. Currently, because underlying goods are not strong, the overall market is dull and stable.

Flour: Near-Term Decline, Long-Term Rise 199

Yesterday, the flour market opened in the morning without price fluctuations, remaining unchanged until the afternoon. The current month was weak due to ongoing sales and a lack of investor confidence, with most transactions being closing positions. However, distant months rose because inland buyers generally believed that after the sudden hot weather, the weather would change again, and distant months would therefore become more expensive. As a result, customer sentiment turned strong, and buying interest was very active, causing prices to remain high. As a result, the current month was down 0.25 cents compared to the previous day, May and June were up 0.75 cents, July was up 1 cent, August was up 1 cent, and September was up 0.75 cents.

Far-Term Wheat: Inland Buyers Are Very Eager 200

Yesterday, futures wheat was lackluster due to slight declines in foreign wheat, and investor sentiment was depressed. The lowest price for June and July was about 0.2 cents lower than the previous day, and other months saw little fluctuation. However, when the afternoon market opened, the current month remained stable, and distant months rallied because inland customers were very eager to buy, gradually buying step by step with their great economic power, so the market recovered from weakness. However, there is ultimately a limit to the market value of new wheat. If prices are raised step by step, it is not appropriate in reality. As a result, the current month was unchanged, June was up 1 cent, July and August were unchanged, and September was up 2 cents. Spot wheat prices were flat and weak because only Fuxin and Lu continued to take over, while other factories remained unchanged. The asking price for Qing, Qian, Pu wheat, Nansu wheat, Yaowan wheat, and Bengbu wheat was 5.1 yuan, Shashi wheat was 4.87 yuan, and 4.77 yuan, totaling 4,000 bags.

Foreign Rice: Weak in the Morning, Strong in the Afternoon 201

Yesterday morning, foreign rice was very weak due to the arrival of spot goods and the weak market sentiment from the previous day. Then, customers from the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway and Jiangbei and other guilds made inquiries, and the market turned from weak to strong. Although prices did not rise or fall, the market atmosphere was already tight. For futures, various inland guilds inquired, but foreign firms did not sell due to the holiday. The market only squeezed about 1,000 tons of the current month at a price of 7.16 yuan, which was a new transaction. There were also more than 1,000 tons of returned goods, but the market improved by one or two cents because foreign firms did not sell and inland customers inquired.

Soybean Market Continues to Weaken 202

Yesterday, the soybean market continued to weaken, with successive declines in contract prices and sluggish sales. Oil mills were also slow to purchase due to poor oil sales, with only small mills and workshops making slight inquiries. Inland guilds also watched and waited because transportation was not cost-effective due to low inland prices. Only two cars of Ping Ge Lian Yuan were opened, priced at 5.412 yuan, while the standard was also 0.2 cents lower, opening at 0.41 yuan. The market was flat and weak.

Silk and Tea: Tunxi Tea and Dexing Tea Recent News 203

▲ Tunxi Tea Firms Are Not As Lively As In Previous Years

▲ Dexing Tea Firms Cannot Open Due To Banditry

▲ Tunxi: The annual export volume of Anhui's Tunxi green tea is about 120,000 chests or more. There are about 70 or more tea firms. Although it was burned and looted by Zhu bandits last spring, the losses of tea merchants were relatively small. The original tea firms were able to open in time and did not decrease. Unexpectedly, the impact of the Russian Association's suspension of Chinese tea affected the unsold Gongxi Zhenmei chest tea stored in Shanghai last winter. Most ended with more losses than profits. This year's new tea will soon be on the market. The number of Tunpu tea firms preparing to open is not as lively as in previous years. In addition, due to sluggish financial conditions and high prices, most of the tea firms are waiting and watching, and the market is showing a rather bleak scene.

▲ Dexing: Gan Province's Dexing is a rich tea-producing area. No less than 30,000 chests of tea are produced each year. Gaozhuang Zhenmei is sold for more than 100 taels. Merchants in the area are gradually becoming more aware of the importance of operating foreign green tea, and the number of tea firms is also increasing year by year. However, it has been ravaged by communist bandits in recent years. Most of the tea leaves cannot be picked and processed in time, and production has declined. Although some people ventured to operate in Dexi, Haikou, and Huanshui last year, they all suffered losses. This year, the tea firms in Dexing dare not prepare to open because the remaining bandits are still lingering and have not been cleared, and it is difficult to handle the transportation of tea funds. The canning factory established in Germany last year has now moved to Taibai in Wujing. Tea firms with ample capital are even more reluctant to operate. If the bandit atmosphere does not subside next month, the Dexing tea market may disappear invisibly.

▲ The YMCA Declares: The Advanced Wireless Electricity Specialty School of this Association has been established for several years. The chairman of the department, Mr. Wang Xun, has now held a meeting to discuss and assign broadcasting work. Business News 205

▲ The China Industrial Bank Declares: This bank has been established for many years with sufficient capital and well-known credit. Therefore, business is developing day by day. ▲ As summer is approaching and the weather is getting hotter, all kinds of seasonal medicines will be launched in turn. This year's Donghuo Mudan's wholesale price has increased sharply due to the rising gold price. This has a considerable impact on the cost of sales. Those who sell this product are all afraid of losing money, and they all hold a wait-and-see attitude. However, the medicinal power and efficacy of Shengdan produced by Jiufu Company in this city are not inferior to a certain Mudan. As it is completely a domestic product, this year's wholesale price has not only not increased at all, but also newly established ordering methods have increased the interests of various sales companies. In addition, the company does not hesitate to sacrifice and set up a one-yuan trial sales method, so that merchants in remote towns and villages can also sell it. This move has greatly increased the sales power of various sales families. Therefore, those who order and try to sell Shengdan in various places have recently sprung up like mushrooms, and the company is working day and night to catch up. This is good news for the future of domestic products and is also welcome by those who promote health.

▲ Shunfeng Stockings Factory Declares: The factory's stockings are an outstanding product in the domestic knitting industry. Among domestic products, there is no one better than it. In the past, the products of this factory were sold through other companies, so they could not trade directly with customers. Now, in order to meet the needs of society, this factory has specially set up the first sales outlet at No. 547 Qipan Street, north of the Sanmao Pavilion Bridge.
